## V48 ‚Äî The UV-editor texture backdrop is the same READ-ONLY DISPLAY PROJECTION as the UV layout (a V33 sibling), resolved by ONE pure producer-aware resolver; its vertical orientation follows the texture's `flipY` so the texel a UV vertex samples sits BEHIND it

**The invariant:** the UV editor's base-color texture backdrop (UX-BACKLOG #10) is NOT a new data path ‚Äî it is the SAME discipline as the UV layout (V33): a read-only display projection of render-side state, extracted by ONE pure function `resolveMeshTexture` (the sibling of `resolveMeshUVs`), sync where possible and NON-throwing where async (status `loading`, never a Suspense throw ‚Äî the panel is not inside a Suspense boundary). The panel and the `__basher_uv_texture` side-B seam read THROUGH that one resolver, so they never drift (the [[H40]] boundary-pair rule). The producer-aware branches mirror `resolveMeshUVs` exactly: glTF/GltfChild/GltfAsset ‚Üí the loaded clone's `material.map` (sync once registered); BakedMesh ‚Üí the baked material's `map` ref; Box/Sphere ‚Üí the inline material's `maps.albedo` ref ‚Äî the two baked paths peeked from the baked-texture loader via the new NON-throwing `peekBakedTexture` (cache hit ‚Üí texture, miss ‚Üí kick off load + null, cached decode error ‚Üí null, NEVER throw/hang).

**The registration sub-rule (the part that is easy to get backwards):** the UV editor draws an island vertex `(u,v)` at screen `(ox+u¬∑sz, oy+(1-v)¬∑sz)` ‚Äî a V-up display flip. For the texel a vertex samples to appear BEHIND that vertex, the backdrop's vertical orientation must follow the texture's `flipY`: `flipY=true` (OpenGL/three default ‚Äî UV(0,0)=image **bottom-left**) ‚Üí draw **upright**; `flipY=false` (glTF/DirectX ‚Äî UV(0,0)=image **top-left**) ‚Üí draw **flipped** (`translate(ox, oy+sz); scale(1,-1)`). The resolver reports `flipY`; the draw side applies the conditional. Observed proof (Lokayata, 64√ó64 asymmetric albedo fixture, green marker at the image's TOP-LEFT): with a glTF `flipY=false` map the green corner lands at screen BOTTOM-LEFT = UV(0,0) ‚Äî exactly where glTF sampling places it. Real cicada (100MB glb, 706 children): a textured child resolves its 1024√ó1024 atlas and the islands register over it.

**Breaks when:** the backdrop is drawn at a FIXED orientation instead of reading `flipY` ‚Üí a glTF map (flipY=false, the common case) appears vertically mirrored relative to its islands; the resolver THROWS on an async miss (e.g. calling `resolveBakedTexture` instead of `peekBakedTexture`) ‚Üí the panel, which has no Suspense boundary, crashes white; a decode failure is not caught ‚Üí the editor blanks instead of falling back to the grid (the `peekBakedTexture` error-cache ‚Üí null path is the resilience guarantee); the seam reads a DIFFERENT path than the panel ‚Üí side A/B drift (the [[H40]] trap the ONE-resolver rule prevents). **Known limitation (by design):** a multi-material asset has many textures but the whole-asset backdrop shows only the FIRST base-color map ‚Äî registration is exact only for a single-material CHILD selection (Blender shows one active image too). Type: STRUCTURAL (read-only projection + orientation). Sibling of [[V33]] (UV layout is a read-only projection), [[V29]] (resolver purity), cross-refs [[H40]] (boundary-pair seam).

**Enforcement (SHIPPED 2 slices on `ux-overhall`):** E2E `tests/e2e/ux10-uv-texture.spec.ts` (2): a glTF base-color map ‚Üí the side-B seam reports `ok`/64√ó64/`flipY=false` for both the whole asset and the textured child; a mesh with NO base-color map (default BoxMesh; a metallic-roughness-only quad) ‚Üí `none`, no backdrop (grid-only path intact). Unit `src/app/asset/bakedTextureLoader.test.ts` (3): `peekBakedTexture` returns null on a miss (not a thrown promise) + kicks off exactly one load; fills in once decoded; a decode failure keeps peek null forever while the Suspense core `resolveBakedTexture` still re-throws for its error boundary. Files: `src/app/resolveMeshTexture.ts` (the ONE resolver), `src/app/UVEditor.tsx` (the dimmed flipY-aware backdrop + header Texture toggle), `src/app/asset/bakedTextureLoader.ts` (`peekBakedTexture`), `src/app/boot.ts` (`__basher_uv_texture` seam), `public/assets/albedo-textured-quad.gltf` (the asymmetric verification fixture). Decisions: base-color/albedo map (Blender default), UV0, dimmed backdrop (globalAlpha 0.6) + on/off toggle; an opacity slider + map picker are open follow-ups, not built (no observed friction). Status: **IMPLEMENTED.** Branch `ux-overhall`.

---

## V49 ‚Äî Keyframe interpolation is ONE shared core: explicit handles ‚Üí real cubic B√©zier, NO handles ‚Üí the exact legacy linear/smoothstep (render parity); the curve editor SAMPLES THROUGH that core so the drawn curve IS the played curve

**The invariant:** there is exactly one keyframe-sampling implementation (`src/nodes/keyframeInterp.ts`, `sampleScalarKeyframes` / `sampleVec3Keyframes`). A segment whose bounding keys carry explicit `inHandle`/`outHandle` evaluates a true cubic B√©zier (solve b√©zierX(s)=t by bisection, then b√©zierY(s)); a segment with NO handles takes the EXACT pre-#11 branch (linear lerp, or smoothstep when the destination key's easing is 'cubic'). This guarantees saved animations render byte-identically ‚Äî and it is provably exact, not approximate: flat B√©zier handles at ¬±span/3 reduce to smoothstep (equally-spaced X control points ‚Üí b√©zier-X linear in s ‚Üí the Y polynomial collapses to a+(b-a)¬∑s¬≤(3-2s)). Vec3 shares ONE time-handle across components, so the x‚Üís solve runs once and per-axis projection (`projectAxis`) matches `segmentVec3` exactly. The curve editor (`EditableCurve`) draws its polylines by calling the SAME core ‚Äî so what is drawn is what the renderer plays (the [[H40]] display-side rule; a divergent local sampler is the bug this replaced ‚Äî the old read-only CurveEditor had its own smoothstep that drifted from the evaluator the moment handles were wired).

**Breaks when:** a consumer re-implements interpolation instead of calling the shared core (the curve drawn diverges from the curve played ‚Äî H40); a no-handle segment is routed through the B√©zier path with a floating-point x‚Üís solve instead of the legacy branch (saved-animation parity drifts by ULPs ‚Äî keep the no-handle branch literal); a B√©zier handle's time extent is left unclamped so X becomes non-monotonic (the x‚Üís solve has multiple roots ‚Üí the curve stops being a function of time ‚Äî the editor clamps each handle to its own half-segment); a Vec3 handle is treated as per-axis-independent in TIME (it is per-axis in VALUE but shares ONE time offset ‚Äî projecting per-axis with the shared time is what keeps the editor curve == the evaluator curve). Type: STRUCTURAL (one sampler + render parity). Sibling of [[V33]] (read-only display projection ‚Äî the curve editor is one), [[V24]] (function-of-time channel value), cross-refs [[H40]] (boundary-pair: the seam/panel sample the same path), [[H48]]/[[H49]] (channel cache stability).

**Enforcement (SHIPPED 3 slices on `ux-overhall`):** unit `src/nodes/keyframeInterp.test.ts` (10 ‚Äî parity: no-handle == legacy linear/smoothstep; the flat-handle==smoothstep proof; asymmetric handle bends; x‚Üís solve for non-uniform time handles; vec3 per-axis with shared time handle) + `src/nodes/nodes.test.ts` (handles survive the zod parse and bend `sample()` through the node `evaluate`). E2E `tests/e2e/ux11-curve-editor.spec.ts` (3): a Vec3 channel draws three non-empty b√©zier `curve-track-*`; dragging a key dot UP raises that component in the DAG (a move, count unchanged); dragging the OUT handle writes an explicit handle (time>0) and reshapes the curve. Render parity proven end-to-end by the unchanged p7 rotation-delta motion gate + p153 boundary-pair. Files: `src/nodes/keyframeInterp.ts` (the core), `src/nodes/KeyframeChannelNumber.ts` / `KeyframeChannelVec3.ts` (delegate), `src/timeline/EditableCurve.tsx` (the reze-style graph editor ‚Äî draws + edits through the core), `src/timeline/CurveEditor.tsx` (mounts EditableCurve for authored Number/Vec3). reze-studio is the visual reference (single-canvas dopesheet+curve; Basher uses SVG for the small-N channel case). Decisions: AskUserQuestion 2026-06-15 (start with the curve editor; wire real cubic-b√©zier). Status: **IMPLEMENTED (curve editor + reze-fidelity dopesheet + shared zoom/pan via [[V50]]).** Branch `ux-overhall`.

## V50 ‚Äî The dopesheet (canvas) and the curve editor (SVG) are two surfaces that share ONE view model: zoom/scroll live in `timelineViewStore`; both map time‚Üíx through `timelineView.frameToX`, and at the default view frameToX === keyframeToRect (parity)

**The invariant:** there is exactly one timeline-view state ‚Äî `{ zoom‚â•1, scroll‚àà[0,1] }` in `src/timeline/timelineViewStore.ts` (a `valueZoom` for the curve's value axis lives alongside it). Both the dopesheet canvas and the SVG curve editor read it, so switching the Dopesheet|Curve tabs holds the SAME visible frame window (the UX-#11 "unify" ‚Äî kept as two tabs sharing a view, NOT one merged canvas; user decision 2026-06-15). The time‚Üîx math is ONE pure module (`src/timeline/timelineView.ts`: `frameToX`/`xToFrame`/`visibleFrames`/`zoomAtFrame`/`panByPixels`). Each surface passes its OWN gutter/track-width/inset; only zoom+scroll are shared, so a given view shows the same frame range on both even though pixel origins differ. **The parity sub-invariant (e2e safety):** the dopesheet bakes the diamond edge-inset into frameToX so that at `{zoom:1,scroll:0}` frameToX reproduces `timelineCanvasGeometry.keyframeToRect` EXACTLY (same affine map: inset + (frame/total)¬∑(width‚àí2¬∑inset)). That is why the geometry-pinned e2e (p7.1, p7.12) and the cull contract (p6-w9) survive the zoom refactor unchanged ‚Äî only zoom>1 / scroll>0 introduce new behaviour. The playhead also goes through frameToX (rAF, view read via `getState()` ‚Äî still zero React render, V20), so it lines up exactly with the diamond at its frame.

**Breaks when:** a surface re-derives time‚Üíx with its own zoom math instead of `timelineView` (the two tabs drift out of sync ‚Äî the seam that V50 prevents); the default-view inset is dropped from the dopesheet's frameToX (default geometry shifts by the inset ‚Üí p7.1/p7.12 drop the diamond they grab ‚Äî see the parity proof in `timelineView.test.ts`); the r–êF playhead reads a closure-captured `view` instead of `getState()` (stale zoom after a wheel ‚Äî D-W9-3 stale-closure trap); auto-scroll writes the view from the rAF every frame (continuous setView ‚Üí the dopesheet static-layer cache repaints every frame ‚Üí the D-W9 bottleneck the cache exists to avoid ‚Äî auto-scroll, if added, must page-jump on threshold, not scroll continuously). Type: STRUCTURAL (one view model + render parity). Sibling of [[V49]] (one shared sampler), [[V34]] (one substrate), [[V8]] (file-rooted UI store). Cross-ref [[H95]] (e2e mirror the geometry constants ‚Üí must update in lockstep when geometry changes).

**Enforcement (SHIPPED 3 slices on `ux-overhall`):** unit `src/timeline/timelineView.test.ts` (10 ‚Äî visibleFrames at zoom 1/2/clamp; the **keyframeToRect parity proof** at the default view; frameToX/xToFrame round-trip across zoom/scroll; zoomAtFrame anchor-preservation; panByPixels bounds). E2E `tests/e2e/ux11-dopesheet.spec.ts` (ruler-scrub drives time; time-zoom culls off-window keys via `data-rendered-keyframes`). Default-view parity proven by p7.1 + p7.12 + p6-w9 passing UNCHANGED. Files: `timelineView.ts` (pure math), `timelineViewStore.ts` (shared store), `TimelineCanvas.tsx` (dopesheet: paint/playhead/hit-test/scrub/wheel through the view), `EditableCurve.tsx` (curve: timeToX/xToTime/sampling/ruler + Shift-wheel value zoom), `boot.ts` (`__basher_timeline_view` K12 seam). Interactions: Ctrl/‚åò-wheel = time zoom anchored on playhead; plain wheel = pan; Shift-wheel = value zoom (curve only). Deferred: auto-scroll, box/multi-select, quat/color curve, clip-row shared view. Status: **IMPLEMENTED.** Branch `ux-overhall`.

## V51 ‚Äî A camera's lens (focal length + sensor) and depth of field reduce to ONE pure mapping each, and `fov` stays the single rendered source of truth; the live viewport and the offscreen still consume the SAME settings ‚Üí bokeh/framing match

**The invariant:** the DAG stores a camera's `fov` (three.js vertical degrees) as the rendered truth; the inspector PRESENTS focal length (mm) + sensor size and derives FOV through ONE pure module (`src/app/cameraLens.ts`: `focalLengthFromFov`/`fovFromFocalLength`, clamped to the schema [1,170]). Depth of field likewise: director params (`dofEnabled`/`focusDistance`/`fStop`) + the lens map through ONE pure module (`src/app/cameraDof.ts` ‚Üí `DepthOfFieldEffect` `worldFocusDistance`/`worldFocusRange`/`bokehScale`). BOTH the live viewport (`PostFx` `<DepthOfField>`) and the offscreen still (`renderToImage` imperative `DepthOfFieldEffect`) build the effect from that one helper's output, so the live bokeh equals the rendered bokeh (the V37/V47 parity pattern extended to the camera). `fov`/`near`/`far` already flow to the editor view (look-through + free orbit), the frustum helper (`CameraHelpers`), and the production render (`buildRenderCamera`) ‚Äî no second camera pipeline (V34).

**Breaks when:** focal length is stored as a second source of truth alongside fov (they drift; keep fov canonical, derive focal); the viewport and render compute DoF settings with different formulas (bokeh mismatch ‚Äî both MUST call `resolveCameraDof`); `sensorSize` (a defaulted authoring param, not consumed by the renderer) is read without a `?? 36` default (pre-#12 projects ‚Üí NaN focal ‚Äî the V10/H14 two-layer guard); a derived FOV is written without `clampFov` (zod re-validation throws on dispatch). Type: STRUCTURAL (one mapping, one source of truth, two consumers). Sibling of [[V37]]/[[V47]] (viewport‚Üîrender parity), [[V34]] (one substrate), [[V49]]/[[V50]] (one shared pure core).

**Enforcement (SHIPPED, UX-BACKLOG #12, 2026-06-15, branch `ux-overhall`):** unit `src/app/cameraLens.test.ts` (round-trip, monotonicity, clamp, guards), `src/app/cameraDof.test.ts` (monotonicity: lower f-stop ‚Üí bigger bokeh + shallower range; longer lens ‚Üí bigger bokeh; resolveCameraDof null when off / non-perspective). E2E `tests/e2e/ux12-camera-lens.spec.ts` (Camera section + focal‚Üífov‚Üílive-view) + `tests/e2e/ux12-depth-of-field.spec.ts` (the DoF render differs from no-DoF by >1000 px ‚Äî falsifiable parity). Files: `cameraLens.ts`, `cameraDof.ts`, `CameraLensControls.tsx`, `PerspectiveCamera.ts` (params), `inspectorSections.ts` (camera section + routing), `PostFx.tsx`/`renderToImage.ts`/`renderImageAction.ts`/`SceneFromDAG.tsx` (the two consumers). Status: **IMPLEMENTED.**

## V52 ‚Äî Exactly ONE component owns the main-scene render each frame; in Basher that is `PostFx`'s EffectComposer (priority-1 useFrame). Any other priority-positive frame callback must OVERLAY (clear depth only), never re-render the main scene

**The invariant:** R3F skips its auto-render when any `useFrame` has positive priority (`internal.priority > 0`), and runs priority subscribers in ascending order (highest renders last ‚Üí on top). Basher's beauty pass (`PostFx`, `src/render/PostFx.tsx`) drives a postprocessing `EffectComposer` at `useFrame(cb, 1)` ‚Äî it is the SOLE owner of the main-scene render (RenderPass ‚Üí EffectPass[DoF, SMAA, ToneMapping] ‚Üí screen). Every other priority renderer must be a pure OVERLAY at a HIGHER priority that clears depth only and composites on top ‚Äî e.g. the orientation gizmo `<GizmoHelper renderPriority={2}>` (drei `<Hud>`: at priority ‚âÝ 1 it skips its `gl.render(mainScene)` branch and only draws the gizmo scene).

**Breaks when:** a second component renders the main scene at priority 1 (drei `<Hud renderPriority=1>` ‚Äî the GizmoHelper default ‚Äî does exactly this; it re-renders the raw scene every frame and DISCARDS the composer's post-processing ‚Üí SMAA/ACES/DoF silently vanish, no error ‚Äî see [[H96]]); PostFx is NOT mounted while a priority-positive overlay is (nothing renders the main scene ‚Üí black/stale); two composers both render to screen (wasted GPU + ordering races). Diagnostic when post-fx "does nothing": log `state.internal.subscribers` priorities in a `useFrame` ‚Äî more than one positive-priority renderer of the main scene is the smell. Type: STRUCTURAL (single render owner). Sibling of [[V20]] (rAF reads `getState()`, zero React render), [[V37]] (one beauty pass, viewport == render).

**Enforcement (SHIPPED, UX-BACKLOG #12 slice 2, 2026-06-15):** `PostFx` imperative composer (we own the EffectPass ‚Äî drei's child-reading EffectComposer resolved to ZERO passes in this fiber/drei combo, which is what hid the bug for so long); `Viewport.tsx` `<GizmoHelper renderPriority={2}>`. Observed: enabling DoF blurs the live viewport AND the gizmo still overlays; DoF-off renders crisp. Status: **IMPLEMENTED.**

## V53 ‚Äî An imported glTF material reduces to the SAME OpenPBR IR as a native material, captured PRODUCER-side (at import, from JSON) onto the addressable node; the renderer OVERLAYS it onto the clone preserving textures; absent ‚Üí clone's embedded material

**The invariant:** glTF embedded materials are not a second material model. They reduce to the one OpenPBR `InlineMaterialSpec` (`openpbrMaterialSchema`, the core-10 lobes) ‚Äî the same IR `BoxMesh`/`SphereMesh` carry inline ‚Äî so one inspector editor, one `openpbrToThree` compile target ([[V32]]), one serialization path apply to both. Capture happens PRODUCER-side at import (`buildGltfImportOps` reads `json.materials[]`, NOT the rendered three.js clone ‚Äî the importer builds the DAG, [[V34]]; the renderer must never write material data INTO the DAG). Each `GltfChild` carries an OPTIONAL `materials: InlineMaterialSpec[]`, one per mesh primitive (slot) in primitive order. The renderer (`GltfAssetR`) maps each clone slot ‚Üí its GltfChild via the nearest stamped ancestor ([[V44]] by-id, exported `nearestChildId`) + a per-child primitive counter, then OVERLAYS the IR's scalars onto a CLONE of the imported material (`overlayDagMaterial`) ‚Äî **preserving the clone's texture maps** (capture seeds `maps:null`; texture capture is a later slice). Because the captured scalars ARE the glTF's own factors, re-applying them onto the still-textured clone is IDENTITY for an unedited import (colour √ó map is how glTF composites) ‚Üí pixel parity.

**Breaks when:** capture reads the render-time clone instead of import JSON (renderer‚ÜíDAG write ‚Äî boundary violation, re-render loop; rejected option B); the overlay REPLACES the material instead of overlaying (strips the clone's textures ‚Äî the maps=null regression the overlay-not-replace rule prevents); the slot‚Üîchild mapping uses NAME not the stamped id ([[V44]]); a colour captured in the wrong space (glTF factors are LINEAR; the IR is sRGB hex ‚Äî convert via three's `Color`, matching GLTFLoader); a missing `materials` is treated as "no material" rather than "fall back to clone embedded" (breaks pre-#178 saves, [[V10]]/[[H14]]). Type: STRUCTURAL (one material model; producer-side capture). Sibling of [[V32]] (renderer-agnostic IR), [[V34]] (one substrate, producer builds it), [[V44]] (by-id across the import‚Üîclone boundary), [[V37]] (viewport == render).

**Enforcement (SHIPPED S1‚ÄìS4, #178, 2026-06-16, `ux-overhall`):** `gltfMaterialToOpenpbr.ts` (clone‚ÜíIR oracle, S1); `gltfJsonMaterialToOpenpbr.ts` + `GltfChild.materials` + `buildGltfImportOps` capture (S2); `overlayDagMaterial` in `SceneFromDAG.tsx` (S3); `GltfMaterialEditor` in `NPanel.tsx` ‚Äî the editable lobe editor routed in for a GltfChild that carries `materials` (S4). Observed: cicada renders pixel-identically; editing `materials[0].base.color` repaints the clone (`tests/e2e/ux-gltf-material-dag.spec.ts`); editing base.color/metalness IN THE INSPECTOR writes the DAG material AND repaints the clone live, multi-slot child has a slot selector that edits one slot only (`tests/e2e/ux-gltf-material-edit.spec.ts`, 3 tests). **S4 WRITE-PATH NOTE:** `setAtPath` (ops.ts) cannot index into an array (a `materials.0.base.color` path REPLACES the array with `{}`), so a glTF material edit MUST be a WHOLE-`materials`-array replace ‚Äî the editor reads the current array, rebuilds the active slot, dispatches `setParam materials`. Native Box/Sphere use a dotted `material.<lobe>.<field>` path because their material is a single OBJECT param; the glTF array shape forces the divergence. **S4 BACKWARD-COMPAT:** routing gates on `gltfChildMaterials.length > 0` ‚Äî a GltfChild with NO captured materials (pre-#178 save / empty bone like cicada `Axe_mesh`) and the whole-asset GltfAsset keep the read-only `GltfMaterialReadout` (V10/H14; the else branch, covered-by-construction + the GltfAsset readout e2e). **S5 EDIT-LAYER MAPS (SHIPPED, #178, 2026-06-16, `ux-overhall` `1b72ee4`+`d61afbe`+`3184eaf`):** a glTF child material's IR `maps` is a SPARSE EDIT-LAYER on the imported clone, NOT a from-scratch map set (the native-material semantics). User decision (the lighter of two architectures): **null ‚Üí INHERIT the imported texture** (default; the S3 overlay preserves the clone's textures, so an unedited 100MB import pays ZERO re-bake/parity cost); **`CLEARED_MAP` sentinel ‚Üí REMOVE** (a BakedTextureRef with an EMPTY hash ‚Äî round-trips through setParam/save/load yet references no OPFS file; `collectAssetRefs` skips empty hashes); **a real BakedTextureRef ‚Üí REPLACE**. Imported textures keep serializing via the embedded glTF bytes (V41) ‚Äî S5 does NOT re-bake originals. Apply: `src/app/material/gltfMapOverlay.ts` (`applyEditedMaps` + slot‚Üíthree-prop map + a cancellation guard); the `GltfAssetR` overlay effect collects meshes with map edits during its sync traverse and async-loads + applies them after (loads can't run inline), re-cloning from the pristine import each run so revert-to-null restores. Inspector: a Maps section in `GltfMaterialEditor` (`GltfMapRow` per slot: pick/replace ‚Üí `attachMapFromFile`, clear ‚Üí sentinel, revert ‚Üí null) ‚Äî whole-`materials`-array replace like the scalars. **S5 flipY RULE:** `attachMapFromFile` stamps flipY=true (the upload convention native Box/Sphere use); a glTF replacement MUST override flipY=false (the glTF UV convention the imported textures use) or it renders vertically flipped (`3184eaf`). Gated by `gltfMapOverlay.test.ts` (6), `ux-gltf-map-overlay.spec.ts` (clear/restore on a live render), `ux-gltf-map-edit.spec.ts` (replace via the file picker ‚Üí real decode ‚Üí hasMap false‚Üítrue; clear sentinel; revert null). Observed: cube renders dark red (green base √ó red 1√ó1 map). **S6 SHIPPED (#178, 2026-06-16, `ux-overhall` `9e321a5`+`c511913`) ‚Äî serialize round-trip + a11y; #178 CLOSED on S1‚ÄìS5 + S6-A/B, animation DEFERRED to #188.** **Part A (.basher round-trip):** an edited glTF material survives export‚Üíopen self-contained ‚Äî a scalar edit (DAG params), a REPLACED map (BakedTextureRef bytes embed + rehydrate), and a CLEARED sentinel (round-trips as plain data, not embedded). Caught a PRE-EXISTING bundle leak (`9e321a5`, H77 instance): `resolveAssetFiles` keyed its baked-texture lookup by the BARE hash, but a real `BakedTextureRef.hash` carries the ext (`<hash>.<ext>` ‚Äî what `persistTexture` stamps) ‚Äî so the lookup missed and the bytes were silently dropped from EVERY bundle with a baked texture (BakedMesh + primitive maps too). The unit fixtures used a degenerate bare `'deadbeef'` hash that never exercised the ext-bearing shape ([[H98]] degenerate-fixture trap), and `resolveAssetFiles` had ZERO unit coverage. Fix: key the lookup by BOTH the full OPFS filename AND the bare hash (current ext-bearing refs match via the filename; legacy bare-hash refs still resolve via the dir listing). Gated: `resolveAssetFiles` unit tests (ext-bearing / legacy bare / no-file-drop) + the real `<hash>.<ext>` collect fixture + cleared-sentinel case + e2e `ux-gltf-material-bundle-roundtrip.spec.ts` (the V41/H77 falsifier: import ‚Üí edit base.color + replace albedo + clear roughness ‚Üí export ‚Üí DELETE the OPFS bytes ‚Üí open ‚Üí all three survive + clone repaints). **Part B (a11y, `c511913`):** the map-row buttons got slot-specific aria-labels ("Pick albedo map" / "Clear albedo map" / "Revert albedo map to imported" ‚Äî six slots otherwise read identically); each row became a named `role=group` instead of a `<label>` (which associated with the hidden file input ‚Üí clicking the slot/state text spuriously opened the OS chooser); the file input keeps its aria-label; the slot selector's radiogroup/radio/aria-checked were already correct; no new className ‚Üí contrast matrix unaffected. Gated: e2e `ux-gltf-material-a11y.spec.ts` (button names, group, file-input label, radiogroup). **Part C (material-scalar ANIMATION) SHIPPED ‚Üí #188** (v0.7 Phase 3, 2026-06-17 ‚Äî see the [[V57]] #188 enforcement note for the full mechanism: materials surfaced on the evaluated value, a per-frame `applyOpenpbrScalars` overlay in `GltfAssetR` on the generic `overlayChannels`/`nodeChannels` road, diamonds on `GltfMaterialEditor`). Originally DEFERRED (user decision via AskUserQuestion, 2026-06-16): its real cost was an architectural arc, NOT wiring ‚Äî `GltfChild.evaluate()` does not surface `materials` (and `GltfChildValue` is not in the `SceneChild` union), and the renderer reads materials from `node.params` via the S3 overlay, not the evaluated value; animating needs the evaluated value to carry `materials` + the renderer to read the EVALUATED/patched materials + a keyframe channel `paramPath` `materials.<slot>.<lobe>.<field>` + diamond/autoKey on the lobe fields + the [[H40]] evaluated-read in the inspector. GROUNDED NOTE on the [[H40]] crux: the animation APPLY side (`AnimationLayer.patchTarget`‚Üí`writeAt`, AnimationLayer.ts:168) traverses `cur[key]`, which DOES index an array path (`materials.0.base.color`) ‚Äî so once the evaluated value surfaces `materials`, the channel apply works. `setAtPath` (ops.ts:60-79) is the blocker ONLY for the un-animated SOURCE write (it replaces an array with `{}`), which S4/S5 already sidestep with a whole-array replace ‚Äî so a `setAtPath` array-index extension has NO current consumer and was REJECTED for now (speculative generality touching the V42/V43/V8/V20 core). Status: **IMPLEMENTED** (S1‚ÄìS5 + S6 serialize + a11y; animation is its own capability, #188). **S5 known-minor (deferred):** repeated replace leaks the prior loaded texture (shared with the existing clone-per-edit pattern, not disposed); a replacement uses TextureLoader-default wrap, not the imported sampler's wrap; override+edited-map combo is handled (apply to final material) but untested.

**DIRECT-IMPORTABILITY GAP ‚Äî the NEXT milestone (planned, not started; goal: "any glTF with textures + materials directly importable", grounded by a pipeline map 2026-06-20).** The loader is SOLID (`gltfLoaderConfig.ts` ‚Äî self-hosted DRACO + KTX2/Basis + Meshopt; GLB + multi-file `.gltf`/`.bin`/images via the `basher-opfs://` URL modifier, [[V23]]; missing-sibling fail-fast [[H98]]; `AssetErrorBoundary` per-asset). Animations/skins/hierarchy capture fully. Material SCALARS capture to the OpenPBR IR (`gltfJsonMaterialToOpenpbr.ts`: base color+metalness, roughness+ior, clearcoat weight/roughness, transmission weight, emission color+strength). **The CORE gap: texture MAPS are never captured into the IR** ‚Äî `gltfJsonMaterialToOpenpbr.ts` seeds `maps: NULL_MAPS`, so the inspector shows EMPTY map slots even though the clone is textured (the renderer overlays scalars onto the still-textured clone ‚Üí pixels look right, but the maps aren't DAG-addressable/editable, and round-trip relies on re-loading the whole `.glb` bytes, not the IR). Closing the gap = capture each material's texture refs (image URI/index + colorspace + flipY + `texCoord` index) into the IR so a map is first-class. **The full silently-dropped list (each renders WRONG with no warning ‚Äî a direct-importability blocker):** (1) texture maps absent from the IR (above); (2) `alphaMode:'MASK'` parsed but ignored ‚Üí cutout renders opaque (no `alphaTest`); (3) `alphaCutoff` dropped; (4) vertex colors (`COLOR_0`) dropped ‚Üí colored models render monochrome; (5) multiple UV sets (`TEXCOORD_1+`) ignored ‚Üí maps on UV1+ render untextured; (6) `KHR_texture_transform` (offset/scale/rot) dropped ‚Üí tiled/offset textures at identity; (7) `KHR_materials_sheen`/`_volume`/`_specular` dropped ‚Üí cloth/glass/spec wrong; (8) `doubleSided` not read into the IR (matches by luck via the clone, but the DAG can't override side). Grounded execution order (from the map): capture map refs into the IR ‚Üí `alphaMode`/cutoff ‚Üí vertex colors ‚Üí multi-UV ‚Üí KHR_texture_transform ‚Üí the remaining KHR lobes ‚Üí doubleSided. Each is a `gltfJsonMaterialToOpenpbr.ts` capture extension + an `overlayDagMaterial`/renderer apply + an IR-schema slot, with a no-silent-drop principle (an unsupported feature should warn via `assetErrorStore`, [[V38]], not vanish). The IR is renderer-agnostic ([[V32]]) so every capture flows to the future TSL backend free.

**SLICE 1 SHIPPED (texture maps, 2026-06-20, `ux-overhall` `a37b40e`).** Gap (1) closed via the user-chosen LIGHTER persistence path (AskUserQuestion fork b): the importer captures each material's texture slots into the IR as IMPORTED-TEXTURE DESCRIPTORS ‚Äî a `BakedTextureRef` with EMPTY `hash` + the glTF texture index (`gltfTexture`) + colorspace + flipY + sampler wrap + captured `texCoord`. Empty hash ‚áí no OPFS bytes (pixels ride in the embedded `.glb`, [[V41]]); `collectAssetRefs` skips it ([[H77]] shape-walk filters `hash!==''`); the renderer LEAVES the clone's texture in place (INHERIT) ‚áí render byte-identical. `captureChildMaterials` passes `json.textures/samplers`; baseColor/emissive = srgb, normal/MR/ao = linear; glTF packs roughness(G)+metalness(B) on ONE `metallicRoughnessTexture` ‚áí both slots share the index. **THE SENTINEL-DISAMBIGUATION TRAP (new, the >1-attempt risk this slice carried):** a captured descriptor and the [[gltfMapOverlay]] `CLEARED_MAP` sentinel BOTH have `hash:''` ‚Äî opposite meanings (imported=inherit, cleared=remove). Centralized in `gltfMapOverlay.ts`: new `isImportedMap` (`hash==='' && typeof gltfTexture==='number'`), and `isClearedMap`/`hasMapEdits`/`applyEditedMaps` now exclude imported descriptors (so an unedited textured import does ZERO map work). NO consumer hand-rolls the sentinel. Inspector: `GltfMapRow` reads `‚óè imported` (captured) vs `‚Äî none` (genuinely empty) ‚Äî the core "empty slots" symptom fixed. Observed: `gltf-texture-map-capture.spec.ts` boundary-pair (DAG `albedo.gltfTexture:0` side A == clone `hasMap` side B); bundle-round-trip + override-textured + map-edit regression green. vitest 1790. Known-minor: replace-then-revert sets the slot null (`‚Äî none`) not back to the descriptor (render still correct via inherit; the row no longer holds the original ref).

**KEY REFRAMING (grounded 2026-06-20, observe `applyOpenpbrScalars` SceneFromDAG.tsx:1500 + `overlayDagMaterial`:1521) ‚Äî CONFIRMED by observation:** the renderer OVERLAYS captured scalars onto the GLTFLoader clone and writes ONLY a subset (color/metalness/roughness/ior/clearcoat/transmission + now alphaTest/vertexColors/side); it NEVER strips the rest (sheen/volume/specular/iridescence/anisotropy/maps/etc.). So for DIRECT imports essentially EVERY glTF material feature ALREADY RENDERS CORRECTLY via the clone ‚Äî the "silently dropped" list is a REPRESENTATION gap (not DAG-addressable/editable/round-trippable-via-IR + lost only if a from-IR path rebuilds), NOT a render-fidelity bug. Verified: a new `__basher_gltf_meshes` seam (alphaTest/transparent/vertexColors/side) showed cutout (alphaTest=0.5) + vertexColors=true on the clone BEFORE any capture (`gltf-alpha-vertexcolor-capture.spec` side-B passed while side-A failed). This reframing is the milestone's organizing insight: capture-for-representation, warn (don't render-fix) for the rest.

**SLICES 2‚Äì5 SHIPPED (2026-06-20, `ux-overhall` `f7783e6`‚Üí`89750d3`).** Gaps (2)(3)(4)(8) captured into the IR `geometry` lobe (optionals ‚Äî native + pre-milestone byte-identical): alphaMode:'MASK'‚Üí`geometry.alphaCutoff` (`f7783e6`), COLOR_0‚Üí`geometry.vertexColors` (per-PRIMITIVE detect in `captureChildMaterials`, not the material JSON ‚Äî same commit), `doubleSided`‚Üí`geometry.doubleSided` (`c5d5b5b`). Apply path: `openpbrToThree` emits alphaTest/vertexColors/doubleSided (THREE-free booleans); `applyOpenpbrScalars` writes alphaTest/vertexColors/`side` ‚Äî IDENTITY for an unedited import (equals what GLTFLoader set on the clone), editable thereafter (the overlay re-clones on edit so vertexColors/side recompile correctly ‚Üí no needsUpdate churn). Gap (7) KHR lobes + (5) multi-UV + (6) texture_transform ‚Üí NO-SILENT-DROP NOTICE (`89750d3`, fork-3): pure `detectUnsupportedGltfFeatures(json)` reads `extensionsUsed` (catches unknown FUTURE extensions too) + TEXCOORD_1+ scan ‚Üí `GltfImportChainResult.unsupportedFeatures` ‚Üí a CONSOLE notice (NOT the red `asset failed:` banner ‚Äî user decision: the import is faithful, the banner would mislabel + spam on most PBR models; structured list rides the result for a future notice UI). Remaining (5) UV1+ APPLY for DAG-replaced maps deferred. Known-minor: no inspector control yet for alphaCutoff/doubleSided (addressable via setParam, render responds). [[V53]] holds.

**SLICE 6 SHIPPED ‚Äî KHR_texture_transform gap (6) (2026-06-20, `ux-overhall` `cd33e8a`).** GROUNDED in three's GLTFLoader source (`extendTexture`, GLTFLoader.js:2007 ‚Äî sets offset/repeat/rotation about the DEFAULT `texture.center=[0,0]`, the UV ORIGIN, NOT [0.5,0.5] like Basher's native `buildLeafMaterial`). Capture: `gltfJsonMaterialToOpenpbr` reads KHR_texture_transform from a material's texture slots ‚Üí populates the SINGLE SHARED `uvTransform` (tiling=scale/offset/rotation) WHEN uniform across the maps; a per-map-DIFFERING material captures IDENTITY (the clone renders each map's own ‚Äî not broken, just not collapsible into one shared transform). Apply: a NEW `applyGltfUvTransform` (SceneFromDAG, called right after `overlayDagMaterial`) CLONES the overlay material's map textures (A-5 ‚Äî clone-shared) and sets repeat/offset/rotation with center **[0,0]** ‚Üí IDENTITY for an unedited import (reproduces GLTFLoader byte-for-byte), live-editable thereafter (editing `materials.<slot>.uvTransform` re-runs the `[cloned,override,depNodeMap]` overlay effect ‚Üí re-applies). **THE TWO-CONVENTION FACT (catalogue this): glTF/`applyGltfUvTransform` pivots about center [0,0] (UV origin, KHR spec); Basher-native `buildLeafMaterial` pivots about [0.5,0.5] (Blender). Each matches its source's authoring convention ‚Äî do NOT unify them.** Warn reconciliation: KHR_texture_transform ADDED to `SUPPORTED_GLTF_EXTENSIONS` (no longer blanket-flagged); `detectUnsupportedGltfFeatures` now flags ONLY the per-map-differing case via `materialHasPerMapUvTransform`. Seam: `__basher_gltf_meshes` exposes `mapRepeat/mapOffset/mapRotation`. Observed: `gltf-texture-transform-capture.spec` (DAG uvTransform==clone map repeat/offset side A==B identity; edit tiling‚Üí[5,5] repaints live). Fixture `uv-transform-quad`. vitest 1804.

**SPEC/GLOSS SUPPORT SHIPPED (#214, 2026-06-21, `ux-overhall` `30268fe`‚Üí`bb62284`, 5 commits).** The finding below is FIXED: spec/gloss models import textured + correct. THE FIX (user-chosen FULL scope): convert KHR_materials_pbrSpecularGlossiness ‚Üí metal-rough AT INGEST (`ingestGltfFolder`, the disk‚ÜíOPFS write step) ‚Äî the ONE point before BOTH readers of the OPFS bytes (render's GLTFLoader via `useGLTF` AND capture's `buildGltfImportOps` each re-parse the SAME OPFS bytes independently), so one converted source ‚áí render == capture for free ([[V37]]/[[H40]]). A loader-plugin was REJECTED (fixes render only ‚Üí forces a 2nd converter for capture ‚Üí the combined-texture map would exist at render but not in the IR ‚Üí render‚âÝcapture). **Increment 1 (`30268fe`):** pure core `src/core/import/specGlossToMetalRough.ts` ‚Äî the FULL Khronos `solveMetallic` approximation (`specGlossToMetalRough(diffuse,specular,gloss)` shared by the factor AND per-texel paths so they cannot diverge): diffuseFactor‚ÜíbaseColorFactor (via the diffuse/specular lerp by metallic¬≤), diffuseTexture‚ÜíbaseColorTexture (same sRGB color texture, reused index), specularFactor+glossiness‚ÜímetallicFactor/roughnessFactor (roughness=1‚àígloss), strips the ext from the material + `extensionsUsed`/`Required` (else GLTFLoader rejects the required ext). Wired in `importGltf.ts` ingest. **Increment 2 (`4c51405`):** combined `specularGlossinessTexture` (spec RGB, gloss A) per-pixel conversion ‚Äî app-layer `src/app/asset/specGlossIngest.ts` (browser canvas: createImageBitmap+OffscreenCanvas, which pure core can't do) decodes the spec/gloss image, runs `specGlossPixelsToMetalRough` per texel, bakes a metallic-roughness PNG (R=AO white, G=roughness, B=metalness, LINEAR/lossless) written as a NEW glTF SIBLING (a normal image+texture entry in the rewritten JSON + a PNG file next to the .gltf) ‚Äî so render loads it via the ordinary sibling resolver, capture records it as an ordinary imported descriptor, and it round-trips through the `.basher` whole-`user-imports/<folder>` embed (`listFilesDeep`, [[V41]]) ‚Äî NO hash-keyed baked-store / [[H77]] dual-key concern. A diffuse texture (if any) is canvas-resampled to the spec map's size for the per-texel metallic solve; absent ‚Üí the diffuseFactor. Graceful degrade ([[V38]]): an undecodable image (KTX2, bufferView-image, missing sibling) keeps the factor-only conversion, never throws the import. **Increment 3 (`4eedad3`):** committable fixture `public/assets/specgloss-quad.gltf` (TWO spec/gloss materials ‚Äî factor+diffuseTexture AND combined-texture) + boundary-pair e2e `gltf-specgloss-capture.spec.ts` (side A converted metal-rough IR == side B rendered clone maps). **Increment 4 (`2b7f14b`):** no-silent-drop reconciliation ‚Äî a converted .gltf never flags spec/gloss (the ext is stripped, `detectUnsupportedGltfFeatures` reads the converted bytes); spec/gloss reaching the unsupported list ‚áí an UN-converted source (a .glb, DEFERRED ‚Äî three r169 renders it flat-white) ‚Üí a DISTINCT render-WRONG notice with the remedy "re-export as .gltf", not the generic "renders but not editable". **OBSERVED (Lokayata, live gas_station import):** 0/81 textured all-#ffffff ‚Üí **50/81 textured with varied material colors**; captured IR carries albedo maps + roughness 0.6; the combined material `lambert43SG` carries roughness+metalness maps (gltfTexture 40 = the newly-baked map, srgb-linear) rendered on its clone mesh; 0 console errors. 22 core unit tests + 2 e2e; vitest 1834. **KNOWN-LIMITS (v1):** (a) GLB repack deferred (gas_station is .gltf; spec/gloss .glb ‚Üí warn); (b) for a combined-texture METAL, the base color keeps the diffuse (factor/texture) rather than baking a per-texel reconstructed base-color texture ‚Äî fine for dielectrics, the documented approximation gap for coloured-specular metals (glTF-Transform bakes both maps; we bake only MR); (c) the baked MR sibling name is `basher-mr-<materialIndex>.png` (deterministic, V22). Type: DATA-FLOW (a producer-side extension never parsed) ‚Üí RESOLVED at the ingest pre-pass. Catalogued finding (kept for the WHY) below ‚Üì

**SPEC/GLOSS .GLB SHIPPED (#216, 2026-06-21, `ux-overhall` `cc98fd5`‚Üí`48d1c99`, 3 increments).** Closes the #214 known-limit (a): a spec/gloss `.glb` now converts AT INGEST exactly like a `.gltf`, instead of importing flat-gray + warning "re-export as .gltf". The blocker was that Basher had `parseGlb` but no GLB WRITER, so a `.glb`'s converted JSON had no way back into the binary container ‚Äî `ingestGltfFolder` gated conversion on the `.gltf` extension. **Inc 1 (`cc98fd5`):** pure `repackGlb({json,bin})` added to `src/core/import/glb.ts` (the inverse of `parseGlb`, same MAGIC/CHUNK constants/domain ‚Äî glTF 2.0 ¬ß4.4: header + JSON chunk 0x20-padded + optional BIN chunk 0x00-padded). Round-trip `parseGlb‚àòrepackGlb` is identity; 5 unit tests. **Inc 2 (`476527f`):** `convertSpecGlossGlb(entry)` in `specGlossIngest.ts` ‚Äî `parseGlb` ‚Üí `convertSpecGlossDocument` (the SAME pure factor + diffuseTexture conversion, container-agnostic) ‚Üí bakes each combined `specularGlossinessTexture` by reading its source image from the **BIN bufferView** (`resolveGlbTextureBytes` ‚Äî the realistic GLB case the `.gltf` path's sibling resolver couldn't reach) ‚Üí embeds the baked MR map as a **`data:` URI image** (self-contained, no BIN surgery; capture already decodes data URIs) ‚Üí `repackGlb`. The `.gltf` + `.glb` paths SHARE the decode‚Üíbake‚Üíencode math (`bakeMetalRoughPng`) and the JSON wiring (`wireBakedMrTexture`); only image RESOLUTION (sibling file vs BIN bufferView) and MR EMBEDDING (sibling PNG vs data URI) differ. A new extension-dispatching `convertSpecGlossEntry(entry,files)` is the single seam `ingestGltfFolder` calls (the obsolete "re-export as .gltf" warning became a malformed-container fallback). 4 unit tests (pure container + factor path; the canvas bake needs a browser). **Inc 3 (`48d1c99`):** committable `public/assets/specgloss-quad.glb` (generated by `scripts/gen-specgloss-glb-fixture.mjs`) ‚Äî the binary twin of the `.gltf` fixture, crucially storing its combined texture as a **bufferView image in the embedded BIN** (exercises the new resolver) + boundary-pair e2e `gltf-specgloss-glb-capture.spec.ts`. **OBSERVED (Lokayata, real browser, both e2e green):** side A (captured IR metal-rough: SGDiffuse metalness 0 / roughness 0.6 / albedo map; SGCombined baked MR descriptor gltfTexture‚â•2 srgb-linear, factors 1√ó) == side B (the rendered clone carries base + metalness/roughness maps from the embedded data-URI) ‚Äî render == capture, textured not gray. vitest 1851 (+9). **KNOWN-LIMITS (v1):** (i) a GLB referencing EXTERNAL textures (uri, not bufferView/data) ‚Üí combined-bake degrades to factor-only ‚Äî `convertSpecGlossGlb` is self-contained (takes no `files`); rare, and pre-existing GLB+external-sibling territory ([[V66]]), not a regression; (ii) the baked MR rides as a data-URI image (‚âà33% base64 bloat in the JSON chunk) rather than appended to the BIN ‚Äî simpler + self-contained; (iii) combined-texture metal base color keeps the diffuse (same documented approximation as the `.gltf` path, #214 limit b). LESSON (process, not code): `git add -A` in inc 2 accidentally committed the untracked scratch harness `tmp-gas-station-observe.spec.ts` (untracked again via a forward `git rm --cached` in `6a8dab1`, no history rewrite) ‚Äî stage explicit paths, never `-A`, near a known-untracked scratch file. Type: DATA-FLOW + the one-writer discipline. Catalogued finding (kept for the WHY) below ‚Üì

**METAL BASE-COLOR BAKE SHIPPED (#218, 2026-06-22, `ux-overhall` `afce864`).** Closes the #214/#216 known-limit (iii): a combined `specularGlossinessTexture` material kept its DIFFUSE as base color, wrong for a coloured-specular METAL (gold/copper/brass) whose tint lives in the SPECULAR channel ‚Üí the metal rendered near-black. THE FIX: the per-texel `specGlossToMetalRough` core already computes the correct base color (lerps diffuse‚Üîspecular by metallic¬≤); new pure `specGlossPixelsToMetalRoughAndBase` returns the MR map, the reconstructed base-color map, AND `maxMetallic`. The ingest bakes the base map + wires it as `baseColorTexture` (neutralising the RGB factor, keeping alpha) ONLY when `maxMetallic > 0.05` ‚Äî a fully-dielectric material keeps its original diffuse (no extra texture, no canvas re-encode degradation; the existing #214/#216 dielectric fixtures stay BYTE-IDENTICAL + green, proving the gate). Shared by both container paths via the extended `wireBakedMrTexture` + `pushBakedTexture` (MR pushed FIRST so its index stays stable ‚Üí existing assertions hold). OBSERVED: +4 pure core tests (gold‚Üíbase from specular, dielectric‚Üíbase‚âàdiffuse + 0 metallic, peak-metallic, MR back-compat) + a committable gold-metal fixture `specgloss-metal-quad.glb` (solid-gold combined texture via a minimal PNG encoder in the generator) + e2e (captured IR gets a baked sRGB albedo descriptor; clone renders base + metalness maps). vitest 1855. **REAL-WORLD FINDING ‚Äî SPEC/GLOSS glTFs import UNTEXTURED (2026-06-21, FIXED by #214 above ‚Äî finding kept for provenance).** OBSERVED on a live real-world import (`/Users/mrityunjaybhardwaj/Documents/CG/models/gas_station/scene.gltf`, 81 meshes / 74 materials / 40 textures, `extensionsRequired:['KHR_materials_pbrSpecularGlossiness']`): geometry imports perfectly (81 meshes) but **0/81 meshes are textured and every material is `#ffffff`** ‚Äî the model renders as flat gray geometry (screenshot `/tmp/gas-station-import.png`). TWO INDEPENDENT DROPS, both confirmed: (1) **RENDER** ‚Äî three.js REMOVED the spec-gloss `GLTFLoader` plugin at ~r150 (we're on r169; `grep -c pbrSpecularGlossiness three/examples/jsm/loaders/GLTFLoader.js` = **0**), so the clone gets default white `MeshStandardMaterial` for every material AND the diffuse textures are never even loaded; (2) **CAPTURE** ‚Äî `gltfJsonMaterialToOpenpbr.ts` reads ONLY `pbrMetallicRoughness` (`mat.pbrMetallicRoughness ?? {}`), which these materials lack (their data is in `extensions.KHR_materials_pbrSpecularGlossiness`) ‚Üí IR captures defaults (`base.color #ffffff`, `maps: all null`). **This BREAKS the milestone's "clone renders faithfully" reframing ‚Äî it only holds for extensions three STILL supports; an extension three dropped renders NOTHING.** spec/gloss is extremely common (older Sketchfab/Substance/Maya exports), so this is a major direct-importability blocker the synthetic-quad fixtures could not surface. **THE FIX (user-chosen FULL scope, next session): convert spec-gloss ‚Üí metallic-roughness at the glTF JSON level BEFORE `GLTFLoader` sees it ‚Äî ONE conversion point fixes BOTH render (clone reads normal metal-rough) AND capture (`gltfJsonMaterialToOpenpbr` reads `pbrMetallicRoughness` normally).** Mapping: `diffuseFactor/Texture‚ÜíbaseColorFactor/Texture`; `specularFactor`+`glossinessFactor`‚Üí`metallicFactor`/`roughnessFactor` (standard spec-gloss‚Üímetal-rough approximation); strip the extension from `extensionsUsed`/`Required`. FACTOR + `diffuseTexture` case = cheap channel/factor remap. COMBINED `specularGlossinessTexture` (spec in RGB, gloss in A) = per-pixel conversion (canvas readback ‚Üí R=metal-from-spec, G=rough=1-gloss ‚Üí write a new MR texture ‚Üí OPFS-persist). The IR is renderer-agnostic ([[V32]]) so the converted material flows to the future TSL backend free. Observation harness: `tests/e2e/tmp-gas-station-observe.spec.ts` (UNTRACKED scratch ‚Äî drives `__basher_ingestGltfFolder` with the on-disk model + reads `__basher_gltf_meshes`; re-run after the fix to confirm 81/81 textured). Type: DATA-FLOW (a producer-side extension never parsed).

## V54 ‚Äî On project LOAD the editor view frames the scene's bounding SPHERE, with near/far + orbit limits DERIVED FROM the bounds (radius), never fixed constants; the fit is a one-time framing, not a look-at constraint

**The invariant:** when a project boots / is switched-to / opened (`EditorViewCamera`, no captured/saved pose), the editor orbit camera frames the scene's world-space bounding sphere ‚Äî position along the canonical [3,2,3] angle at a fit distance, lookAt = center, near/far + OrbitControls min/max ALL derived from the radius (bounded far/near ratio so a 0.01-unit gem and a 10,000-unit terrain both frame without clipping/z-fighting). Two pure helpers: `fitViewToSphere` (`cameraFit.ts`) consumes `computeSceneBounds` (`sceneBounds.ts`, world-space sphere of non-chrome meshes ‚Äî same editorChrome/TransformControls denylist as the render hide-pass, [[V37]]). Because glTF loads ASYNC (after the boot effect), a `useFrame` SETTLE loop re-fits as the bounds grow and ends ~0.75s (SETTLE_STILL_FRAMES) after the bounds last CHANGED ‚Äî NOT on first stability (a sync box stabilizes in ~2 frames while the model arrives ~0.5-2s later; an early exit frames the box and misses the model). The fit is ONE-TIME: any canvas input (pointerdown/wheel) cancels it and OrbitControls owns the FREE camera thereafter (no per-frame re-pin ‚Äî explicit camera constraints are a future feature). A projection-toggle captured pose and the user's saved orbit view WIN over the fit.

**Breaks when:** planes are fixed constants (0.1/1000) ‚Üí large model clips at far, small at near (the pre-#186 bug); the settle ends on first stability ‚Üí frames the sync box, never re-frames to the async model; the fit keeps re-applying after settle / doesn't yield to input ‚Üí the camera feels pinned to center (explicitly rejected by the user); bounds via `Box3.setFromObject` (recurses into chrome) instead of per-mesh world boxes ‚Üí chrome inflates the frame; the boot guard is lifetime-scoped not (project,projection)-keyed ‚Üí no reframe on in-session switch ([[H69]], #167). **GAP CLOSED (#191, 2026-06-16):** the saved-view & projection-toggle branches now run a PLANES-ONLY settle ‚Äî keep the restored pose, but re-derive near/far + dolly limits from the LIVE camera distance each frame (`clipPlanesForView`, separable from the pose-fit because planes depend on camera distance not fit distance). The shared full-fit math is the single source of truth (`fitViewToSphere` delegates to `clipPlanesForView`). Watch [[H101]]: refreshed dolly limits must be CLAMPED to not exclude the live camera distance, else OrbitControls dollies a restored close pose out to satisfy minDistance ‚Äî a silent re-frame. Type: STRUCTURAL + LIFECYCLE (async settle). Sibling of [[V37]] (chrome denylist), [[V51]] (lens/fov source of truth), builds on #167 (project-keyed boot guard).

**Enforcement (SHIPPED Slices 1‚Äì4, #186, 2026-06-16, `ux-overhall` `cfbdb52`‚Üí`76cc515`):** `src/viewport/cameraFit.ts` (+11 unit) + `src/viewport/sceneBounds.ts` (+6 unit) + `EditorViewCamera.tsx` (boot priority pending>saved>fit, settle `useFrame`, canvas-input cancel, near/far via state for persp AND ortho). Observed (Lokayata): default box boots framed ~[1.88,1.25,1.88] near>0.5/far<50 (not 0.1/1000); a grown 4000-unit box dollies the eye past 1000 with far>2000 no-clip (`p186-frame-all-clip-planes.spec.ts`); `p165` boot‚Üíbounds-fit + frustum-click dollies out + `p167` reframe‚Üíbounds-fit. Open-Scene reframe verified by equivalence (importSceneBundle mints a fresh id+setCurrent = the Duplicate path p167 tests). **#191 SHIPPED (2026-06-16, `ux-overhall` `fa82248`‚Üí`0533082`):** `clipPlanesForView` extracted (+6 unit), saved/pending branches run a planes-only settle, dolly limits clamped to the live distance ([[H101]]); `p191-saved-view-clip-planes.spec.ts` reloads a large-box project with an injected close saved view ‚Üí eye stays at saved pose, far ~4510 (not 1000); p186/p167/spline-projection regression-green. DEFERRED: an on-demand "Frame All" command.

## V55 ‚Äî Viewport-VIEW settings (clip planes) are an editor projection independent of the SCENE camera; the free view clips by an AUTO bounds-fit with an optional per-project manual override, while the scene camera node's near/far drives ONLY the render + look-through

**The invariant:** the editor's free orbit VIEW and a scene CAMERA node are two different things with two different clip-plane sources (the #165 decoupling, generalized). The free view's near/far = `viewportClipOverride ?? autoBoundsFit` (#186/#191) ‚Äî an editor-session projection (`viewportStore`), never the DAG (V8/V34). The scene camera node's `near`/`far` params drive the offscreen RENDER (`renderActiveProjectBlob` reads `cameraPoseFromNode`) and the LOOK-THROUGH preview (`EditorViewCamera` uses `pose.near/far` when `lookThrough`), and NOTHING else. A "viewport clipping" control must therefore live on the VIEW (View ‚ñ∏ Clipping), and editing it must NOT touch any camera node; conversely the camera node's near/far must NOT bleed into the free view. The override is AUTO by default (so the bounds-fit still prevents clipping out of the box) and persists per project to localStorage (`viewportClipPersistence`, the same editor-state class as the editor-view pose ‚Äî NOT the project file). `normalizeViewportClip` is the single validator (near>0, far>near, finite ‚Üí else AUTO) shared by the store setter and the persistence layer.

**Breaks when:** a viewport clip control is wired to the camera node's near/far ‚Üí editing the view changes the render (the conflation the user explicitly rejected: "camera settings should only affect the camera in the scene not the viewport view"); the free view reads `pose.near/far` outside look-through ‚Üí the scene camera bleeds into the editor view; the override REPLACES the auto bounds-fit instead of layering over it ‚Üí large/tiny models clip again by default (regresses #186/#191); the hydration effect uses the persisting setter ‚Üí it echoes the loaded value straight back to localStorage; an invalid pair (near‚â•far) is stored ‚Üí a degenerate frustum (guarded by `normalizeViewportClip` ‚Üí AUTO). Type: STRUCTURAL (boundary: view-projection vs scene-data) + a sibling of [[V54]] (the auto bounds-fit the override layers over) and the #165 view‚Üîcamera decoupling.

**Enforcement (SHIPPED #192, 2026-06-17, `ux-overhall` `527371a`‚Üí`610a861`, 3 slices):** Slice 1 `viewportStore.viewportClipOverride`/`viewportClipReadout` + `normalizeViewportClip` + `viewportClipPersistence` (+12 unit). Slice 2 `EditorViewCamera` free-view effective planes = override ?? auto, settle honors the override, readout published, per-project hydration on projectId change. Slice 3 `MenuBar` View ‚ñ∏ Clipping submenu (Auto / Clip Start‚Ä¶ / Clip End‚Ä¶ via window.prompt, persist on set). Observed (`p192-viewport-clip.spec.ts`): store override ‚Üí `__basher_view_camera` near/far adopts it; clear ‚Üí back to auto; reload hydrates the persisted override; View ‚ñ∏ Clipping ‚ñ∏ Clip End "250" ‚Üí far==250 persisted, ‚ñ∏ Auto ‚Üí cleared + entry removed. Render path never imports `viewportStore` (separation holds by construction). vitest 1636; p186/p191/p165/ux5-menu regression-green.

## V56 ‚Äî A keyframed CAMERA is followed everywhere by ONE pure resolver; its channels target the camera node DIRECTLY (no AnimationLayer), because the camera is wired via scene.camera, outside the scene-child machinery

**The invariant:** the active camera's EVALUATED pose at time T comes from ONE pure resolver `resolveActiveCameraPoseAt(state, seconds)` (`activeCamera.ts`) ‚Äî the static authored base (`cameraPoseFromNode`) overlaid with any `KeyframeChannel*` whose `target` is the camera node, sampled at `seconds` via the SAME shared interp primitives the channel nodes use (`buildVec3Sampler`/`sampleScalarKeyframes` ‚Äî one sampling source, no parallel walk). That ONE resolver feeds all three consumers so they frame the SAME shot at time T (the [[V37]]/[[V51]] viewport==render parity): the live viewport look-through (`EditorViewCamera` samples it each frame from LIVE time+DAG snapshots ‚Äî never a time subscription, [[H48]]), the still render (`renderImageAction` at the playhead), and the animation render (`renderAnimationAction` per-frame inside `capture()`). Camera channels target the camera node DIRECTLY with NO AnimationLayer wrapper ‚Äî the camera is wired via `scene.camera` (a single `Camera`-typed ref), NOT `scene.children`, so the layer machinery (Mesh-typed sockets, `patchTarget` cloning a SceneChild) cannot carry it. The resolver is the camera analogue of `resolveEvaluatedTransform` for scene children; the dopesheet surfaces camera channels via its orphan-channel path (`collectChannelRows`, no layer needed).

**Breaks when:** a consumer reads `cameraPoseFromNode` (static params) instead of the resolver ‚Üí that surface freezes the camera at its authored pose while the others animate (the pre-#190 state: viewport memoized pose on node identity, render read once); the first-key path runs `addLayer` on a camera (the scene-child composite) ‚Üí wraps the Camera in a Mesh-typed AnimationLayer and rewires `scene.camera` to the layer ‚Üí `selectActiveCameraNode` finds the layer (no pose params) + look-through breaks (the [[H104]]-adjacent boundary; fix = `dispatchCameraFirstKey`, a single free-floating channel); the viewport `useFrame` subscribes to time instead of snapshotting it ([[H48]]); held transients are overlaid in the resolver ‚Üí render parity breaks (a render is of committed state ‚Äî transients are a viewport-only concern, intentionally excluded; see #194). Type: STRUCTURAL (one resolver, one sampling source) + the scene.camera-vs-scene.children boundary. Sibling of [[V37]]/[[V51]] (parity), the `resolveEvaluatedTransform` pattern, and #165 (view‚Üîcamera decoupling).

**Enforcement (SHIPPED #190, 2026-06-17, `ux-overhall`, 6 slices):** `resolveActiveCameraPoseAt` + 7 unit (`activeCamera.test.ts`); `renderImageAction`/`renderAnimationAction` consume it (still at playhead, animation per-frame); `EditorViewCamera` look-through follow `useFrame`; `dispatchCameraFirstKey` (camera branch in `dispatchFirstKeyComposite`) + 3 unit; `ParamDiamond` extracted + `CameraLensControls` diamonds/autoKey for fov/near/far ([[H104]]); `collectChannelRows` orphan path surfaces camera channels (locked by test). Observed (`p190-camera-animation.spec.ts`, REAL R3F view camera): inject a position/fov channel ‚Üí look through ‚Üí scrub ‚Üí the view camera dollies to x‚âà12 and fov ramps 20‚Üí80; clicking the REAL inspector fov diamond on the camera creates a free-floating KeyframeChannelNumber with NO AnimationLayer (scene.camera stays wired to the camera). vitest 1647; ux12/p165/p7 regression-green. DEFERRED: animated DoF (#193), held-transient look-through preview + dopesheet camera-row labels + gizmo-on-camera e2e (#194). Status: **IMPLEMENTED.**

## V57 ‚Äî Every animatable node is driven by free-floating direct channels (target = dagId, paramPath) overlaid by ONE pure primitive (`overlayChannels`) that BOTH the renderer and the read-side consume; the `AnimationLayer` wrapper is the legacy holdout being absorbed, not a second animation model

**The invariant:** "animate a node's params over time" reduces to ONE mechanism ‚Äî a free-floating `KeyframeChannel*` whose `params.target` is the animated node's dagId and `params.paramPath` is a dotted band into its value, overlaid by the ONE pure primitive `overlayChannels(base, channels, weight, seconds)` (`src/nodes/overlayChannels.ts` ‚Äî `patchTarget` lifted out of the `AnimationLayer` node, clone base ‚Üí `writeAt(paramPath, blend(sample(seconds)))`). The SAME primitive is consumed by BOTH the renderer (a per-node `useFrame` overlay at the live time SNAPSHOT) AND the read-side resolver (gizmo/inspector at `ctx.time`), so displayed == rendered (the [[H40]] "one band, two callers"). The camera (`resolveActiveCameraPoseAt`, [[V56]]) and glTF transform (`resolveGltfChildTrs` + `bakedGltfChannels`) are pre-existing instances of this road; v0.7 (#195) generalizes it to native meshes via `src/app/nodeChannels.ts` (`directChannelNodesForTarget` / `channelValuesFromNodes` / `directChannelTargetSet` ‚Äî channel values built through each node's OWN `evaluate`, one sampling source) + `DirectChannelsR` (render) + the `resolveEvaluatedTransform` overlay (read). `AnimationLayer` is NOT a second model ‚Äî it is a re-parenting wrapper carrying only `mute` + (number/vec3) `weight` (its solo/boneMask/cross-layer are declared-but-inert, `AnimationLayer.ts:88-92`); its `patchTarget` IS this primitive, and it is being absorbed (Phase 5 retirement + the authoring switch).

**Breaks when:** a by-target channel enumerator does NOT exclude channels wired into an `AnimationLayer.animation` socket ‚Üí during coexistence the node double-overlays (the channel is applied by BOTH `AnimationLayerR` and the direct path) ‚Äî the [[H105]] coexistence trap; the renderer overlays but the read-side does not (or vice-versa) ‚Üí the gizmo/inspector freeze at the authored pose while the viewport animates (the #68/#77 displayed‚âÝrendered class, [[H40]]); the per-node render subscription is NOT narrowed (shallow on the channel node refs) ‚Üí an unrelated edit re-renders every animated node (the [[H48]]/B13 storm ‚Äî the fix is `directChannelTargetSet` built once + a stable boolean prop so static nodes' memo bails); the `useFrame` subscribes to time instead of snapshotting it ([[H48]]); a literal reading "absorb the primitive ONTO glTF" makes a native mesh a non-producer (loses parametric geometry) ‚Äî the unification is at the animation/override layer ONLY, the primitive keeps PRODUCING its geometry. Type: STRUCTURAL (one mechanism, one overlay primitive, two callers). Sibling of [[V56]] (camera instance), [[V53]] (one material IR ‚Äî the band material flows through), [[V20]] (one precedence rule), [[H40]] (two callers).

**Enforcement (#188 SHIPPED, v0.7 Phase 3, 2026-06-17, `ux-overhall` `e258cea`‚Üí`2f2de8f`, 3 commits ‚Äî the THIRD direct-channel consumer family: glTF MATERIALS).** glTF child material scalars/colours now animate end-to-end on this road. (1) `overlayChannels` GENERALIZED to a generic `<T>` over the base shape (was `SceneChild`-only) so it overlays a `GltfChildValue` carrying `materials` ‚Äî it already indexed the `materials.<slot>.<lobe>.<field>` array path, so NO `setAtPath` change (V53). (2) `GltfChild.evaluate()` surfaces `materials` + `gltfAssetDepNodes` subscribes material channels (Number/Color, `paramPath` starts `materials.`, `target ‚àà nodeNameMap` values). (3) The renderer animates via a NEW per-frame `useFrame` in `GltfAssetR` ‚Äî the material analogue of the TRS useFrame: the override EFFECT establishes the cloned materials (structural), the useFrame overlays the sampled scalars onto those LIVE materials each frame via the extracted no-clone `applyOpenpbrScalars` (ONE field-mapping source shared with `overlayDagMaterial`); re-cloning per frame would churn GC (the SAME reason TRS writes `child.position.set`). Slots a MaterialOverride tint/flatten claims are recorded `null` (not animation targets ‚Äî composing channel-over-override defers to Phase 4). (4) Still + animation render follow for FREE (no render-path code) ‚Äî both capture the LIVE scene (`renderSceneToImageCanvas` `gl.render(scene)`) and the animation render advances per-frame via `setTime`+`waitForApply` so the live `frameloop="always"` useFrames apply before capture (unlike the CAMERA, which is outside useFrame and needed an explicit per-frame resolver in #190). (5) Authoring: `dispatchCameraFirstKey` GENERALIZED to `dispatchDirectFirstKey({allowed,‚Ä¶})` ‚Äî camera (number/vec3) AND a NEW GltfChild branch (number/color) both create a free-floating channel targeting the node directly; `GltfMaterialEditor` renders a `ParamDiamond` per lobe field + an autoKey-aware `commit` ([[H104]] ‚Äî a custom control must re-wire the diamond/autoKey spine). The material-channel enumerator's [[H105]] layer-wired guard is a documented NO-OP (a GltfChild is never layer-wrapped ‚Äî not a scene producer). Gated: `GltfChild.test` + `gltfAssetDeps.test` (Slice 1, +7 unit), `p188-gltf-material-anim-boundary-pair.spec.ts` (rendered metalness ramps 0‚Üí0.5‚Üí1, base.color tracks ‚Äî REAL `__basher_gltf_meshes`), `p188-gltf-material-authoring.spec.ts` (diamond ‚Üí free-floating channel, ZERO AnimationLayer). vitest 1678; p190/ux-gltf-material-edit/p7.13 regression-green. **SEAM A SHIPPED ‚Äî LIGHTS now render their animation (#212, 2026-06-21, `ux-overhall` `babd0ad`).** A light animated by a free-floating channel now RENDERS, closing the last per-type render-overlay gap. ## V58 ‚Äî Constraints and modifiers are ONE pattern: an ordered, non-destructive chain of TYPED operators over a base value (Houdini SOP/CHOP/VOP); the "parent" is the existing `NodeDefinition` + typed sockets, NOT a new base class; a relationship (aim/track/follow) is DERIVED via a pure resolver from a `target`, never a stored rotation [IMPLEMENTED ‚Äî epic #201: CHOP/constraints #204 + SOP/modifiers #209; epic #235: IMAGE effects #inc2a (`4a6702f`) ‚Äî the SAME `operatorStack.ts` engine now serves `Image‚ÜíImage` video effects (ColorCorrect) via `EFFECT_NODE_TYPES`, predicate-parameterized core + byte-identical geometry wrappers, NO new stack engine. THIRD value type on ONE abstraction (Transform/Mesh/Image). #inc2b (`f934231`): the effect's params keyframe via the SAME [[V57]] free-floating channels + `useAnimatableField`/`ParamDiamond` the 3D inspector + layer props use (H104, targeting the effect node) ‚Äî the operator's params are first-class animatable, not a separate keying road.]

**The invariant:** "transform geometry" (modifier / SOP) and "constrain a transform" (constraint / CHOP) reduce to the SAME shape ‚Äî a linear sub-chain in the DAG where each operator's input is the previous operator's output, presented as a _stack_ (add/remove/reorder/mute). They differ ONLY in the value type on the wires: `Mesh`/`Geometry` (modifiers) vs `Transform` (constraints). The unifying parent is NOT a new class above SOP/CHOP/VOP ‚Äî it is the universal node interface `NodeDefinition<Params,Value>` that EVERY node already implements (the same realization as Houdini, where SOP/CHOP/VOP are all just nodes differentiated by port type, and as Blender's depsgraph, which is itself a DAG). The ONE new shared abstraction is `OperatorStack` ‚Äî chain wiring + stack UI + mute/bypass + serialization + agent op ‚Äî _polymorphic over the value type_, instantiated as a transform stack and a geometry stack. A relationship constraint (Track-To) computes orientation purely from `(position ‚Üí target)` where `target` is a point OR a node-ref (read of the target's pure world transform), NEVER a baked rotation kept in sync (the camera's `lookAt`/[[V56]] is the pre-existing instance; the camera migrates onto Track-To to delete its special-case). VOP = the OpenPBR parametric IR ([[V32]]/[[V53]]) ‚Üí TSL/WGSL later; an arbitrary shader node-graph is deliberately deferred.

**Breaks when:** someone builds "a constraint system" and "a modifier system" as two subsystems ‚Üí the chain wiring / stack UI / serialization / mute / agent op are duplicated (the right move is ONE `OperatorStack` over two value types); someone designs a base class ABOVE SOP/CHOP/VOP ‚Üí ceremony over the thing (`NodeDefinition`) that already unifies them; a constraint stores a baked rotation instead of deriving from a target ‚Üí it freezes/desyncs when the subject or the light moves (the friction Blender constraints exist to remove); a constraint reads the target's WORLD transform from the downstream scene-composition (`SceneFromDAG`) instead of a pure evaluable value ‚Üí viewport ‚âÝ offscreen render ([[V37]] break) and it can't run in pure eval (THE foundational gate, slice #202); the constraint target is NOT modeled as a DAG input edge ‚Üí you re-implement topological ordering + cycle detection that the evaluator (`src/core/dag/evaluator.ts`) already provides for free; the full Blender ~25-constraint list is built before the stack + world-transform model are proven (north star ‚âÝ v1 scope). Type: STRUCTURAL (one substrate, one stack abstraction, typed per category). Sibling of [[V56]] (camera aim ‚Äî the first constraint consumer + the migration proof), [[V57]] (operators are animatable channels for free), [[V32]]/[[V53]] (VOP = the material IR), [[V37]] (render parity ‚Äî every operator + resolver is pure).

**Enforcement:** PARTIAL ‚Äî the gate + the first constraint are IMPLEMENTED. Design captured in `docs/OPERATORS-AND-LIGHTING-DESIGN.md` (commit `51fb46d`); tracked under epic #201, slices #202‚Äì#209. The foundational precondition (primitives + glTF unified onto one `EvaluatedMesh` + one `resolveEvaluatedTransform` band, [[V57]]) is DONE. **#202 ‚Äî world-transform-as-a-pure-value ‚Äî DONE (`48f1c17`/`484740c`): `src/app/resolveWorldTransform.ts`; invariant [[V59]].** **#204 Track-To ‚Äî general mesh constraint DONE (`366f11d`/`2d2edc6`/`cab0e1f`): pure aim (`resolveTrackTo`) + `TrackTo` node + scene-layer resolution (`nodeConstraints.ts`) + render (`ConstrainedR`) + read (`resolveEvaluatedTransform`); invariant [[V60]]. The camera-`lookAt` migration onto Track-To (`fe62ca6`/`033e6d3`) is DONE ‚Äî the camera's bespoke aim is deleted; it's now a normal Track-To consumer (`resolveActiveCameraPoseAt` derives `lookAt` via the shared resolver). #204 COMPLETE.** A KEY DESIGN REFINEMENT learned here: a RELATIONSHIP constraint canNOT be the doc's ¬ß2.2 "wrapper sub-chain" node ‚Äî the aim needs the object's WORLD position, which a bare `evaluate` lacks ‚Äî so relationship constraints resolve at the scene layer (the `resolveActiveCameraPoseAt`/[[V56]] pattern), edge-less + enumerated like channels ([[V57]]); the wrapper-sub-chain model still fits geometry/value operators (SOP). **#209 ‚Äî SOP/modifiers ‚Äî DONE (`2f0537e` operator + `f7e2bbf` OperatorStack + `9304876` UI + `fdd4886` agent op): the geometry half of V58 is now IMPLEMENTED.** A geometry modifier (`ArrayModifier`) IS the doc ¬ß2.2 wrapper sub-chain node the constraint refinement said geometry operators WOULD fit ‚Äî confirmed: a modifier consumes its source mesh VALUE (never world position), so it is edge-WIRED (`Mesh target ‚Üí out`), UNLIKE the edge-less Track-To. The deferred #203 `OperatorStack` was LIFTED here (the 2nd operator consumer earned it) ‚Äî but the #204 refinement collapsed the doc's "polymorphic over transform+geometry": constraints resolve edge-LESS at the scene layer, so the transform stack is NOT a sub-chain ‚Äî `OperatorStack` (`src/app/operatorStack.ts`) serves the GEOMETRY stack only ("one sub-chain helper for the operators that ARE sub-chains"). New invariant [[V64]] (the modifier substrate). Status: **IMPLEMENTED ‚Äî both halves: #204 (CHOP/constraints, [[V60]]) + #209 (SOP/modifiers, [[V64]]). The OperatorStack + agent op + stack UI are the ¬ß2.2 "one new abstraction".**

## V59 ‚Äî Accumulated WORLD transform is a PURE evaluable value (`resolveWorldTransform`) that MIRRORS the `SceneFromDAG` nesting; any surface needing world-space reads it off-graph, never the live scene graph [IMPLEMENTED ‚Äî #202]

**The invariant:** The world transform of any node is a pure function of `(DAG state, time)` ‚Äî `resolveWorldTransform(state, nodeId, ctx)` (`src/app/resolveWorldTransform.ts`) ‚Äî NOT a value composed downstream by three.js at render. It walks the SAME evaluated value tree `SceneFromDAG` renders, in parallel with the DAG input structure (Transform/MaterialOverride ‚Üí `inputs.target`; Group ‚Üí `inputs.children`), multiplying each level's local matrix `T¬∑R(deg‚Üírad,'XYZ')¬∑S` exactly as three.js composes `Object3D.updateMatrix` (`compose(position, quat-from-Euler('XYZ'), scale)`) ‚Üí bit-equal world matrix. The top-level child is overlaid (free-floating channels ‚Üí held transient) the SAME way `DirectChannelsR` renders it ([[V57]]/[[H40]] one band), so an animated ancestor moves descendants' world transforms in lockstep with the render. This is the [[V58]] ¬ß4.3 gate: a constraint reads its target's world transform as this pure value. It is the world-space sibling of `resolveEvaluatedTransform` (local TRS) and `resolveActiveCameraPoseAt` ([[V56]], camera pose) ‚Äî the "one pure resolver per read-need" family.

**Breaks when:** a surface reads world-space from the live three.js scene graph (`object.getWorldPosition` / `updateWorldMatrix`) instead of the resolver ‚Üí it can't run in pure/offscreen eval and viewport ‚âÝ render ([[V37]] break); the resolver's local-matrix composition diverges from what a renderer emits for a kind (e.g. forgetting BakedMesh renders at identity scale because the transform is baked into verts, or using BoxMesh `.size` ‚Äî geometry args ‚Äî as the transform scale instead of `.scale`) ‚Üí silent world drift; the Euler order or deg‚Üírad differs from the renderer's `rotation={degVec3ToRad(...)}` ('XYZ') ‚Üí rotation-only drift a translation test misses; the top-level overlay is dropped ‚Üí an animated parent's children freeze in the resolver while the render moves (the displayed‚âÝrendered [[H40]] class). Type: STRUCTURAL+DATA-FLOW (pure-value parity with the render composition). Sibling of [[V37]] (render parity), [[V58]] (the operator/constraint substrate this gates), [[V56]] (camera pose resolver), [[V57]] (the channel overlay it reuses), [[H40]] (one band, no parallel walk).

**Enforcement:** IMPLEMENTED. `src/app/resolveWorldTransform.ts`; unit suite `src/app/resolveWorldTransform.test.ts` (9 tests ‚Äî top-level==local, nested translation/rotation/scale, Group identity, MaterialOverride pass-through, animated-ancestor tracking at ‚â•2 times, identity-null); boundary-pair e2e `tests/e2e/p202-world-transform-boundary-pair.spec.ts` proves resolver world (side B, `__basher_world_transform`) == REAL rendered object world (side A, `__basher_mesh_world_position`) for a nested + animated Transform‚ÜíBox at 2 playhead times. Boot seam `__basher_world_transform` (`src/app/boot.ts`). **#210 GENERALIZED the resolver to ALL node kinds (the renderable-node unification, `1d23e1f` lights + `b579312` camera, 13 unit tests):** a LIGHT is wired flat into `scene.lights` (or the active rig's `scene.lightRig.lights`), so its world == its own `localMatrix` overlaid with the SAME channel‚Üítransient band (mirrors the renderer's `lightRefs[i]`/`rigLightSources[i]` index-correspondence); a CAMERA (wired via `scene.camera`, never in the walks) resolves via an early branch from its pose ‚Äî position + look-orientation (-Z ‚Üí lookAt, the frame `CameraHelpers` draws) + identity scale, position/lookAt channels overlaid by the shared primitive. The camera branch stays INLINE (importing `activeCamera` would cycle: activeCamera ‚Üí `resolveTrackToTarget` ‚Üí resolveWorldTransform) and does NOT reflect a camera Track-To aim (that is the active-camera RENDER path). Observed: `p210-world-transform-any-node.spec.ts` ‚Äî a static light's seam world == the REAL rendered RectAreaLight (H40 boundary-pair); a camera's seam world == `n_camera.params.position` (both were null before). SCOPE still out: GltfChild world (by-name inside an asset) + Scatter-instance/Character-bone world (descent stops; returns null ‚Üí caller falls back). NOTE: an animated light's seam world tracks while the rendered light is still static ‚Äî the SAME resolver/render divergence the inspector has (`resolveEvaluatedParam` tracks, render doesn't); the render catch-up is the separate "lights animate" item (seam A / DirectChannelsR for `LightNode`). Status: **IMPLEMENTED ‚Äî uniform across mesh / light / camera (#210).**

## V60 ‚Äî A relationship constraint (Track-To) DERIVES orientation from a target every evaluation, resolved at the SCENE LAYER (edge-less + enumerated, never a stored rotation); render and read apply the SAME aim [IMPLEMENTED ‚Äî #204 mesh]

**The invariant:** Track-To aims a node so its -Z faces a target (point or node-ref), and the orientation is DERIVED from `(objectWorldPos ‚Üí targetWorldPos)` via the ONE pure resolver `resolveTrackTo` ([[V58]] ¬ß4.1) ‚Äî NEVER a baked rotation kept in sync. Because the aim needs the constrained object's WORLD position (and the target's), which a bare node `evaluate` cannot reach (it has no ancestor context), a relationship constraint is NOT a wrapper sub-chain node (the doc ¬ß2.2 model ‚Äî that fits geometry/value operators). It is EDGE-LESS and enumerated from the node table (`nodeConstraints.ts`), and RESOLVED at the scene-resolution layer (the `resolveActiveCameraPoseAt`/[[V56]] pattern) where `resolveWorldTransform` ([[V59]]) supplies both world positions ‚Äî Track-To is V59's first consumer. The SAME derived aim is applied by BOTH the render (`ConstrainedR`) and the read side (`resolveEvaluatedTransform`) ‚Üí gizmo/inspector show exactly what renders ([[H40]] one band, two callers). No cycle risk: `resolveWorldTransform` is constraint-free (pure TRS), so reading the object's or target's world never re-enters constraint resolution (A‚ÜîB mutual tracks each resolve off the other's un-aimed world).

**Breaks when:** a constraint stores a baked rotation instead of deriving it ‚Üí it freezes/desyncs when the subject or target moves (the friction constraints exist to remove, [[V58]]); a relationship constraint is built as a wrapper node computing aim in `evaluate` ‚Üí it has no world context and the aim is wrong under any parent; the render applies the aim but the read side doesn't (or vice-versa) ‚Üí displayed‚âÝrendered ([[H40]]); `resolveWorldTransform` is made to apply constraints ‚Üí infinite recursion on mutual tracks; the aim Euler order / -Z convention diverges from the renderer's `rotation={degVec3ToRad(...)}` ('XYZ', -Z toward target) ‚Üí silent orientation drift the camera migration would inherit. Type: STRUCTURAL+DATA-FLOW (derived-not-stored; scene-layer resolution; render==read). Sibling of [[V58]] (the substrate), [[V59]] (world transform it consumes), [[V56]] (the camera aim it generalizes + will absorb), [[V57]] (edge-less enumerated, like channels), [[V37]]/[[H40]] (render parity, one band).

**Enforcement (#204 mesh-constraint SHIPPED, 2026-06-19, `ux-overhall` `366f11d`‚Üí`2d2edc6`‚Üí`cab0e1f`):** `resolveTrackTo` (pure aim, 5 unit ‚Äî axis-aligned/arbitrary/camera-convention-matches-Matrix4.lookAt/degenerate-null/moving); `TrackTo` node + `'Constraint'` socket type + `ConstraintValue` + `'constraint'` section + registerAll; `nodeConstraints.ts` (`trackToForTarget`/`constraintTargetSet`/`resolveConstraintRotation`, 9 unit ‚Äî enumeration/point/node-ref/MOVING-target/cycle-safety/mute); read-side fold-in `resolveEvaluatedTransform`; render `ConstrainedR` (SceneFromDAG, per-frame aim with an H48 result-changed guard) + `__basher_mesh_world_quaternion` seam. Observed (`p204-track-to-boundary-pair.spec.ts`, REAL render): a box's rendered -Z (side A, world quaternion) tracks a MOVING target == the read resolver (side B) == the physical target dir, +X@t0 / +Z@t2; falsify by muting ‚Üí -Z stops tracking. vitest 1672‚Üí1686; p202/p149 render-path regression-green. SCOPE: the aim writes LOCAL rotation (correct for a TOP-LEVEL node, identity wrapper); nested constrained nodes (parentWorld‚Åª¬π¬∑aimWorld) + GltfChild/Scatter/Character targets are out-of-scope (V59 scope). v1 is one constraint per node (first-wins); a chain/stack is the `OperatorStack` slice.

**Camera migration SHIPPED (`fe62ca6`/`033e6d3`, 2026-06-19):** the camera's bespoke aim is deleted ‚Äî `resolveActiveCameraPoseAt` now derives `lookAt` from a Track-To via the SAME `resolveTrackToTarget` meshes use (extracted shared `aimTargetWorld`). The camera expresses the aim as a lookAt POINT (Object3D.lookAt == the Matrix4.lookAt resolveTrackTo runs) ‚Äî one constraint system, one aim resolution, each consumer's native form (mesh = Euler, camera = point). No camera Track-To ‚Üí channel/static lookAt stands, byte-identical (no-constraint path returns null pre-eval). Per-frame look-through resolve uses a stable `EvaluatorCache` (content-hash HIT, no per-frame re-walk). 4 unit (node-ref/moving/point/muted incl. byte-identical regression) + e2e `p204-camera-track-to.spec.ts` (REAL look-through camera forward tracks a moving target == constraint, observed). vitest 1690.
