Slice 0 `7c10b43` (`roll` param on both camera nodes + `CameraValue` + `CameraPose`/`cameraPoseFromNode`/`DEFAULT_CAMERA_POSE` + `ANIMATABLE_CAMERA_SCALAR_PARAMS` + the V56 resolver overlay; defaulted ‚Üí no migration; +1 unit). Slice 1 `875cb07` (`cameraOrientation.ts` forward+inverse + 5 unit; `frustumQuaternion`/`applyView`/`buildRenderCamera`/`cameraWorldMatrix` all delegate; `up` added to the `__basher_view_camera` seam; OBSERVED roll 90¬∞ banks the look-through up from [-0.30,0.90,-0.30] to [0.707,0,-0.707], aim unchanged). Slice 2 `770b9a5` (`CameraGizmo` + dispatcher branch + `roll`‚Üítransform inspector routing; e2e `p229-camera-aim-gizmo.spec.ts` 2/2 REAL R3F: aim handle ‚Üí DAG lookAt + look-through agree; rotate ‚Üí aim orbits at fixed distance + roll banks + look-through matches). Gate tsc0/eslint0/vitest **1927**; regression p190/p204/p230 green. KNOWN-LIMITS (v1): the `roll` inspector row shows STATIC `params.roll` during scrub of an animated roll (the [[H104]]/#194 camera read-side caveat ‚Äî `resolveEvaluatedTransform` returns null for a camera, same as position/lookAt today); in translate mode the body + aim handles are both translate gizmos (visually similar ‚Äî distinct in rotate mode); a rotate drag emits lookAt+roll as 2 ops/frame (many undo entries, same as SingleGizmo); roll is gimbal-unstable when aiming near straight up/down (matches Blender's Track-To note); the gizmo seeds via a per-seed render-root `resolveActiveCameraPoseAt` (cache-share follow-up). DEFERRED ‚Üí #234.

## V78 ‚Äî Every scene object speaks ONE socket type ('SceneObject'); a Group/Scene `children` socket holds mesh, light, OR camera, and consumers discriminate on `value.kind` ‚Äî the DAG type system does NOT grow a per-kind socket, and connect-validation stays strict (the types converge, the rule does not loosen) [IMPLEMENTED ‚Äî #231 Inc 1; foundation for groupable/parentable lights & cameras]

**The invariant:** Basher mirrors Blender's "everything is an Object" by giving every scene-object producer (every mesh ‚Äî Box/Sphere/Baked/Modified/Gltf/Transform/Group/MaterialOverride/Scatter/Character/modifiers; every light; every camera) the SAME output socket type `'SceneObject'`, and every scene-graph consumer (`Scene`/`Group` `children`, `lights`, `camera`, `Transform`/`MaterialOverride`/modifier `target`, `Scatter` `assets`, `LightRig` `lights`, render-pass `camera`) accepts `'SceneObject'`. The runtime counterpart is the value union `SceneObject = SceneChild | LightValue | CameraValue` (`src/nodes/types.ts`); the renderer / outliner / selection ALREADY switch on `value.kind`, never on the socket type, so a unified socket needs NO per-consumer growth ‚Äî this is the explicit anti-pattern the old `types.ts` header warned against ("richer variants without the DAG type system needing to grow"). The connect-time check (`ops.ts` `inputDesc.type !== outputDesc.type`) is UNCHANGED: it is still strict string equality ‚Äî the fix is that the type STRINGS converge to one, not that the rule loosens (the rejected "multi-type union socket" fork). A `'SceneObject'` is therefore STILL rejected by a genuinely different socket (e.g. `lightRig:'LightRig'`), proving validation is intact. The change is byte-identical for saved projects because `hydrate()` (`store.ts`) sets DAG state DIRECTLY with no socket re-validation, and a saved edge is a `{node, socket}` ref that carries NO type ‚Äî so renaming a socket-type string is zero-migration (R1, proven).

**Breaks when:** a future scene-object node ships with an output type other than `'SceneObject'` ‚Üí it cannot enter a `children` socket (the gap this closed, re-opened for that node); a consumer branches on the SOCKET TYPE string to tell a light from a mesh (instead of `value.kind`) ‚Üí it silently mishandles the now-unified socket; someone "fixes" the looseness by re-splitting the socket into per-kind types ‚Üí grouping/parenting of lights & cameras breaks again (the rejected fork); the connect rule is loosened to a set-membership/`accepts[]` instead of equality ‚Üí an incompatible producer (Material/Channel) silently connects (the negative test guards this); a node that needs a SPECIFIC kind (a geometry modifier wanting a mesh, a render pass wanting a camera) assumes the socket guarantees it ‚Äî post-#231 the socket only guarantees "a scene object", so the kind must be checked in `evaluate` (transitional looseness, accepted Q-A; resolved when Inc 4 flattens). The superseded `'Mesh'`/`'Light'`/`'Camera'` `SocketTypeName` members are now zero-referenced (kept with a "superseded" comment per Chesterton; prune with Inc 4). Type: STRUCTURAL (one socket type, N producers, value.kind discrimination). Sibling of [[V44]] (correspondence by stable id, never name ‚Äî the band addressing lights-in-children must keep), [[V34]] (one substrate, no parallel store), [[V63]] (LightRig ‚Äî the grouping precedent, stays its own band by design). Enables #231 Inc 2 (groupable/parentable lights & cameras) + Inc 3 (multi-camera `CameraSelect`).

**Status:** IMPLEMENTED (#231 Inc 1, 2026-06-23, `ux-overhall` `3df286c`). `'SceneObject'` added to `SocketTypeName` (`src/core/dag/types.ts`) + `SceneObject` value union (`src/nodes/types.ts`); all 25 scene-object node defs repointed from `'Mesh'`/`'Light'`/`'Camera'` ‚Üí `'SceneObject'`. NO behavior change this increment ‚Äî the renderer keeps its three bands (lights / rig-lights / children) and reads `value.scene.lights/.camera/.children` separately; the type-layer is the foundation Inc 2/3 build on. Gate tsc0/eslint0/vitest **1932** (+5 `src/nodes/sceneObjectSocket.test.ts` ‚Äî light‚ÜíGroup.children + camera‚ÜíScene.children now connect [were `type mismatch` before], mesh + light bands unbroken, `lightRig` still rejects a SceneObject). OBSERVED live: `p197-direct-channel-render` green (meshes + lights + direct channels render unchanged). Design: `docs/BLENDER-DATA-MODEL-PARITY-231-DESIGN.md`. KNOWN-LIMITS (this increment): lights/cameras are TYPE-eligible for `children` but the renderer does not yet RENDER them when nested (Inc 2); `Scene.lights`/`Scene.camera` now loosely accept any SceneObject (Q-A transitional; Inc 4 flatten resolves).

**Inc 2a ‚Äî groupable/parentable LIGHTS (IMPLEMENTED, `b9a77d3`+`7ea7bf9`, 2026-06-23).** The first BEHAVIORAL consumer of the unified socket. 2a.1 (`b9a77d3`): `GroupValue.children` widened to `readonly SceneObject[]`; `MeshChild` gains light kind cases ‚Üí `LightKindR` (a nested light inherits the group's WORLD from `GroupR`'s `<group>` nesting ‚Äî the SAME three.js composition the #202 mesh boundary-pair validates; render == resolver, H40). The world resolver needed NO change ‚Äî its scene-child `walk`/`childEdges`/`localMatrix` already descend `Group.children` and handle a light's TRS, so a nested light's world AND its gizmo parent world (#230) resolve through the existing path. 2a.2 (`7ea7bf9`): top-level lights now PROJECT as outliner rows (`buildSceneTreeRows` walks `scene.lights`, parent.socket `'lights'`); kind-aware reparent (`SceneTree.canReparent`/`reparentSocket`) ‚Äî a light drags into a Group's `children` and back to `scene.lights` (its rich home band). OBSERVED: `p231-grouped-light` (a rendered light at the group-composed world [6,0,0] == resolver, via new read-only `__basher_light_world_positions` seam) + `p231-light-reparent` (DAG + rendered light follows the group). KNOWN-LIMITS (v1): a nested light renders STATIC ‚Äî its direct-channel animation / Track-To aim / viewport helper stay on the top-level `scene.lights` band (the channel/constraint NODES still exist in the DAG ‚Üí no data loss; reparenting back restores them); nested CAMERAS render nothing yet (frustum-at-world = Inc 2b, which shares the camera-pose-under-parent machinery with Inc 3).

## V79 ‚Äî The active camera is resolved THROUGH a `CameraSelect` (when one feeds `Scene.camera`) to the active camera NODE by index; a directly-wired camera is the fallback; the value side (`CameraSelect.evaluate`) and the id side (`selectActiveCameraNode`) clamp the index with ONE shared helper so render == resolver on which camera is live [IMPLEMENTED ‚Äî #231 Inc 3.1; the multi-camera "active" model]

**The invariant:** Basher mirrors Blender's per-scene active-camera pointer with a `CameraSelect` node (the ClipSelect/LightProfileSelect/LightRig [[V63]] switch pattern): N cameras fan into `CameraSelect.cameras` (a `'SceneObject'` list), the single `active` param (an INDEX, Q-B locked) picks one, and the single output feeds `Scene.camera`. `selectActiveCameraNode` (`src/app/activeCamera.ts`) is the ONE chokepoint every camera consumer flows through (editor look-through, SceneFromDAG frustum marker, still/animation render, and `resolveActiveCameraPoseAt` which calls it internally) ‚Äî so making IT resolve through the `CameraSelect` lights up all of them at once. The id-side recovery reads `inputs.cameras[active].node` by EDGE ORDER ([[V44]] index-correspondence), and BOTH the value side (`CameraSelect.evaluate`) and the id side normalize `active` with the SAME `resolveCameraSelectIndex(active, count)` clamp (empty‚Üínull, round + clamp to [0,count-1]) ‚Äî so the CameraValue the evaluator returns and the NODE the resolver picks always agree on which camera is live (H40, render==resolver). `active` is a normal param ‚Üí keyframeable ([[V57]]): `selectActiveCameraNode(state, seconds)` samples a `KeyframeChannelNumber` targeting the select node's `active` paramPath, so a keyframed `active` CUTS the rendered/look-through pose at the frame (Blender's Bind-Camera-to-Markers, but animatable). A camera wired DIRECTLY to `Scene.camera` (every pre-change project, and single-camera scenes ‚Äî lazy auto-insert means CameraSelect appears only on the 2nd camera) is returned unchanged: CameraSelect is additive/optional, zero migration.

**Breaks when:** the value side and id side clamp `active` differently (e.g. one rounds, one truncates; one returns null on empty, one returns index 0) ‚Üí the rendered camera value disagrees with the pose/frustum NODE ‚Üí "the wrong camera renders" with no error (the shared `resolveCameraSelectIndex` + the value-side/id-side mirror tests guard this); the id side recovers the camera by NAME or by scanning `state.nodes` instead of `inputs.cameras[active].node` edge order ‚Üí reordering cameras silently re-points active ([[V44]] violation); a new camera consumer reads `Scene.camera`'s wired node DIRECTLY instead of calling `selectActiveCameraNode` ‚Üí it sees the `CameraSelect` node (not a camera) and breaks pose reads (the chokepoint discipline ‚Äî add consumers THROUGH the selector); `resolveActiveCameraPoseAt` calls `selectActiveCameraNode(state)` without `seconds` ‚Üí a keyframed cut does NOT apply at render time (the pose freezes on the static-active camera). Type: STRUCTURAL (one switch node, one chokepoint resolver, shared clamp). Sibling of [[V63]] (LightProfileSelect ‚Äî the exact switch-by-index pattern), [[V56]] (`resolveActiveCameraPoseAt` ‚Äî the per-frame active-camera pose this feeds), [[V44]] (correspondence by stable id/edge order), [[V57]] (keyframeable param ‚Üí free animation/cuts).

**Status:** IMPLEMENTED (#231 Inc 3.1, 2026-06-23, `ux-overhall` `abdeffb`). `src/nodes/CameraSelect.ts` (node + `resolveCameraSelectIndex`); `selectActiveCameraNode` resolves through it with optional time-aware `active` sampling; `resolveActiveCameraPoseAt` passes `seconds` for cuts. Gate tsc0/eslint0-err/vitest **1951** (+10 `src/nodes/CameraSelect.test.ts` node/clamp + 7 resolve-through in `src/app/activeCamera.test.ts`: fallback unchanged, clamp matches both sides, pose follows active, keyframed cut snaps at t=0.6, static selector ignores the keyframed active). NOT YET (later slices): UI to add a camera / Set Active / outliner camera rows / solid-triangle active marker = Inc 3.2; nested-camera frustum-at-world pose + camera reparent = Inc 3.3. KNOWN-LIMITS (this increment): DoF reads the STATIC-active camera (`selectActiveCameraNode(state)` in render actions) ‚Äî a keyframed cut frames the cut camera but uses the static camera's DoF (consistent with "DoF not yet animatable"); the SceneFromDAG active-frustum marker is static (won't follow a cut mid-playback ‚Äî cosmetic).

**Inc 3.2 ‚Äî the director-facing UI (IMPLEMENTED, `3318a56`+`3cf7548`, 2026-06-23).** `buildSetActiveCameraOps` (`src/app/setActiveCamera.ts`) is the ONE op-builder making a camera active (Blender Ctrl-Numpad0), used by the outliner button, the context item, and the Ctrl-0 shortcut ‚Äî the LAZY auto-insert lifecycle (user-approved): single camera ‚Üí direct wire; 2+ cameras + set-active a non-active one ‚Üí a `CameraSelect` materializes wiring ALL cameras in `enumerateCameraNodeIds` order (the index it addresses, [[V44]]); once present ‚Üí `setParam active` (+ connect if absent). `enumerateCameraNodeIds` (activeCamera.ts) is the ONE camera list the viewport frustums (`SceneFromDAG` now consumes it, de-duped ‚Äî Chesterton), the outliner rows, and the lazy-insert share. Outliner (`sceneTreeWalk`/`SceneTree`): cameras project as depth-1 rows (`parent.socket:'camera'`); the active one shows a SOLID-triangle marker (‚ñ≤), others a hover Set-Active (‚ñ≥); the eye is suppressed on camera rows (it governs only the children band ‚Äî a lying affordance otherwise). `CameraHelper` draws a SOLID FILLED triangle on the active frustum (same 3 verts as the proven wire up-triangle). Camera rows are drag-INERT (`scene.camera` is a SINGLE socket ‚Äî no list reorder; `canDropOn` rejects the `'camera'` socket on both sides) ‚Äî camera reparent is Inc 3.3. +7 `setActiveCamera.test.ts` (each applies ops ‚Üí asserts the resolved active camera) + `p231-active-camera` e2e (rows, marker moves, CameraSelect inserted, resolver follows, Ctrl+0, drag-inert). Gate tsc0/eslint0-err/vitest **1958**. OBSERVED live: outliner active marker moves to the chosen camera (screenshot). KNOWN-LIMITS: nested-camera frustum-at-world pose + camera drag-reparent = Inc 3.3.

**Inc 3.3 ‚Äî FULL nested-camera pose (IMPLEMENTED, `b16f915`+`747e789`+`8370ce0`, 2026-06-23; user chose "full" via AskUserQuestion).** A camera is now a groupable object: nested in a Group, it frames from the group-composed WORLD. ONE composition primitive `composeCameraPoseWithParent(localPose, parentWorld)` (`cameraOrientation.ts`) ‚Äî builds the local orientation matrix, premultiplies parentWorld, reads world (position, lookAt, roll) back via the SAME `cameraOrientationQuat`/`lookAtRollFromQuat` bijection so it renders identically through the point-based lookAt model (worldLookAt == parentWorld¬∑localLookAt for no parent scale, proven). 3.3a (`b16f915`): `resolveParentWorldMatrix` no longer short-circuits cameras ‚Üí the scene-child walk finds a nested camera as a Group descendant (childEdges descends Group.children, V78), returns null for a top-level camera (not in scene.children) ‚Üí byte-identical flat fallback; `resolveActiveCameraPoseAt` composes parent AFTER channel+Track-To overlays (look-through + still + anim render); the world-resolver camera branch composes too (constraints aiming a nested camera); `resolveCameraFrustumPose` lifts each frustum (SceneFromDAG, frame-0 static ctx). 3.3b (`747e789`): camera outliner reparent ‚Äî a camera's "parent" is purely Group.children membership (the active scene.camera edge is independent), `cameraReparent`‚Üí'into'(connect to Group.children, disconnect prior Group)/'root'(unparent nested‚Üífloating top-level); camera rows draggable again, canDropOn still rejects the single 'camera' socket (no reorder). 3.3c (`8370ce0`): gizmo world‚Üílocal write-back ‚Äî the CameraGizmo seeds at world pose (3.3a) so the drag handlers convert back via `parentWorld` captured at seed (`toLocalPoint` for translate/aim; strip parent rotation for rotate ‚Äî the inverse of composeCameraPoseWithParent), null parentWorld ‚Üí #229 direct path byte-identical (the #230/[[H116]] manipulate-in-render-space, store-authored-local pattern, applied to the camera point-model). Proven: +3 composeCameraPoseWithParent unit + 3 nested activeCamera unit + `p231-nested-camera` e2e √ó3 (look-through from world [5,1,0] via `__basher_view_camera`; drag into/out of a Group; gizmo aim at world [5,2,0] under Group@[5,0,0] writes local lookAt [0,2,0]); p229 top-level gizmo 2/2 byte-identical. Gate tsc0/eslint0-err/vitest **1964**. KNOWN-LIMITS: non-uniform parent SCALE shears the camera basis (the #230 limit ‚Äî aim distance preserved, framing exact under translate+rotation); the EditorViewCamera BOOT-framing pose (static `cameraPoseFromNode`, line 136) uses local for a nested camera (cosmetic ‚Äî the live look-through composes); resolveParentWorldMatrix has a cheap O(N) guard (a node referenced by NO hierarchy socket ‚Äî `children`/`target`, the exact childEdges set ‚Äî returns null WITHOUT the render-root evaluate, `36f9e17` self-review), so a top-level camera/light/flat node pays nothing; only a genuinely NESTED node (Group child or Transform target) evaluates (unavoidable ‚Äî it needs the walk). **#231 capability B (multi-camera active) + capability A-cameras (groupable cameras) COMPLETE.** NEXT (optional) = Inc 4 flatten Scene top-level (lights/camera-body into children, resolves Q-A looseness + prunes dead 'Mesh'/'Light'/'Camera' SocketTypeName members); then E (glTF children first-class) = follow-on milestone.

## V80 ‚Äî The 2D View (Blender's Image Editor) is ONE bounded center surface hosting UV + Render Result as persisted tabs; the Render Result renders through the SAME `renderActiveProjectToDataUrl` as the download, and renders in ANY editor space because `renderToImage` targets an explicit offscreen RT ‚Äî valid whenever the Canvas mounted once [IMPLEMENTED ‚Äî unified 2D View, 2026-06-23]

**The invariant:** the editor's `'uv'` space is a unified 2D View (`TwoDView`) ‚Äî Blender's Image Editor model, where ONE 2D area hosts multiple sources picked from a header. Two tabbed modes: **UV** (the existing `UVEditor`, drop-in) and **Render Result** (`RenderResultView`). The active mode lives in `twoDViewStore` (persisted, the `timelineDockStore` clone); both panes stay MOUNTED with the inactive one `display:none` so each canvas + store subscription survives a switch (the same mount-once discipline as the 3D‚Üî2D space toggle and the timeline dock). The Render Result is produced by `renderActiveProjectToDataUrl()` ‚Äî the SAME production-camera offscreen path the "Render Image" download uses ‚Äî so what shows in-pane is byte-identical to what downloads (viewport==render, the [[V37]]/[[V51]] face extended to the in-app viewer). The result is parked in `renderResultStore` (ephemeral ‚Äî a 1080p data URL is megabytes, session-scoped like Blender's unsaved Render Result) so it survives a tab/space switch and so a future fal AI edit writes a new image into the SAME slot (`source:'ai'`, the same data-URL shape `sync_mode` returns). **Render is the Blender F12 verb (`3af3ecb`):** ONE `renderActiveProjectToView()` action ‚Äî switch to the 2D View + Render Result tab, render, park in the store ‚Äî is what the toolbar üì∑, File ‚ñ∏ Render Image, AND the pane's own Render button all call (one verb, one behaviour). It does NOT download; **`downloadRenderResult()` (the "‚¨á Save" pane button) is the separate explicit export** ‚Äî it downloads the data URL currently SHOWN (what you see is what you save, no re-render). Before this, the toolbar/menu Render downloaded immediately and never touched the view, so a user clicking it got a download AND an empty pane ‚Äî the anti-pattern this invariant forbids. Critically, the render works while the 3D `view3d-slot` is `display:none` (the user is in 2D): `renderToImage` renders into an explicitly-sized offscreen `WebGLRenderTarget`, NOT the visible canvas front buffer, so it's independent of canvas visibility ‚Äî the ONLY precondition is that the Canvas mounted at least once so `ThreeBridge` populated `threeRef.gl/scene` (the app boots in 3D, so this always holds before a 2D switch). When it hasn't, `renderActiveProjectBlob` returns null and the pane shows "Viewport isn't ready" ‚Äî the graceful guard, not a crash.

**Breaks when:** a second render entry point reimplements the offscreen render instead of calling `renderActiveProjectToDataUrl` ‚Üí the in-pane result drifts from the download (the ONE-path discipline ‚Äî viewport==render==2D-result); the Render Result is held full-bleed/persisted to localStorage ‚Üí megabytes of base64 in storage, or the image leaks across reloads (it's ephemeral by design); a pane is unmounted on tab switch instead of `display:none` ‚Üí its canvas/scroll/decoded-image is torn down and re-decoded each switch; code assumes the render needs the 3D space ACTIVE ‚Üí it gates rendering on `space==='view3d'` and the 2D Render button no-ops (the offscreen RT is space-independent; only the Canvas-mounted-once precondition matters). Type: STRUCTURAL (one editor surface, one render path, one held-result store). Sibling of [[V37]]/[[V51]] (viewport==render ‚Äî same offscreen path feeds the viewer), [[V46]] (the bounded-center-surface placement it occupies), [[V48]] (the UV-texture backdrop it now hosts under the UV tab), [[V63]] (the persisted tab-switch pattern).

**Status:** IMPLEMENTED (`ux-overhall` `59fccec`, 2026-06-23). `src/app/TwoDView.tsx` (tablist + panes), `src/app/RenderResultView.tsx` (render button + letterbox canvas), `src/app/stores/twoDViewStore.ts` (`mode:'uv'|'render'`, persisted), `src/app/stores/renderResultStore.ts` (ephemeral held result), `src/app/renderImageAction.ts` (`renderActiveProjectToDataUrl` now dual-use: viewer + DEV seam), `src/app/Layout.tsx` (`uv-slot` ‚Üí bounded center surface), label "UV Editor"‚Üí"2D View" in `FloatingViewportToolbar.tsx`+`MenuBar.tsx`. Gate tsc0/eslint0-err/vitest **1964**. Identity transform == the old fit-only draw (byte-identical default); `draw(ctx,w,h,zoom)` gets `zoom` so the UV grid/labels divide by zoom (crisp/constant) while the texture/image scales. ## V81 ‚Äî ComfyUI animation is authored as V57 keyframe channels and RENDERED via the `basher_controller` transport (OUTPUT_IS_LIST); control is always DECLARED ‚Äî author-placed (Mode A) or auto-injected per keyframed foreign param (Mode B) ‚Äî NEVER inferred/rewired; the Basher timeline is the SINGLE source of truth and render==dopesheet via the ONE baker [IMPLEMENTED ‚Äî two-node contract; the legacy inference compiler DELETED 2026-06-30 (task 3); live temporally-coherent clip gated on AnimateDiff models; see Status]

**The invariant (target):** a ComfyUI workflow is ingested into a Basher DAG node (`ComfyGraph` = verbatim API JSON + a derived param manifest); ANY of its literal params becomes animatable by binding a free-floating `KeyframeChannel*` ([[V57]]) targeting the node with `paramPath: comfy:<nodeId>.<inputName>` ‚Äî NO new keyframe machinery (the existing `directChannelNodesForTarget`/`sampleScalarKeyframes` road). On output the keyframes are COMPILED, never left as a per-frame fiction: the **preview** target substitutes baked per-frame values into N independent `/prompt` graphs (fast, any param, but ComfyUI-invisible + incoherent), the **compiled** target bakes each channel to a per-frame array and inserts in-graph schedule nodes (the custom `BasherSchedule` bridge node) + rewires the param's link, so ComfyUI runs the whole animation as ONE coherent batch and the result is a portable, openable ComfyUI artifact. The baker is the SAME `sampleScalarKeyframes`/channel-`evaluate().sample()` the dopesheet + 3D render use ‚Üí preview == compiled == dopesheet (the H40 boundary-pair). The single-frame `ComfySubmitResult` ([[V80]]-adjacent, `ComfyUICapability.ts:44`) is widened with a `submitBatch` for the compiled path; the per-frame `submit` stays for preview.

**Breaks when:** the per-frame fiction is shipped AS "video" (independent runs ‚Üí no temporal coherence + not a ComfyUI artifact ‚Äî the ¬ß2.1 trap the compiled path exists to avoid); a param the compiler can't schedule in-graph (STRUCTURAL ‚Äî checkpoint/resolution/sampler-type, ¬ß7.4) is silently dropped from the compiled path instead of LOGGED + demoted to preview-only (silent truncation reads as "it all animates"); a second keyframe sampler is introduced for workflow params instead of reusing the V57 baker ‚Üí preview/compiled/dopesheet drift; a re-imported workflow's shifted node ids orphan the bound channels without a stable-key rebind ([[V44]] correspondence-by-id, [[H114]] orphan-rebind); the bound channels are stored on the node's params instead of as free-floating channels ‚Üí the NLA can't show them and the V57 road is bypassed; **the COMPILED-path control-pass FEED (`runRenderJob` frame-range‚Üístorage batch) is still the `stubEncoder` 1√ó1 fiction** (Inc-1 current-frame eyeball passes are now REAL per [[V82]]; the per-frame batch feed remains stub ‚Äî Inc 2/3). Type: STRUCTURAL (one source of truth, one baker, two compile targets). Sibling of [[V57]] (the channel road this reuses), [[V44]] (stable-id correspondence ‚Äî re-import), [[V80]] (the Render Result view that previews passes + compiled frames), [[V38]] (surface the demotion ‚Äî no silent no-op).

**Status:** ‚öÝÔ∏è **PIVOTED 2026-06-28 ‚Äî the compiler model is SUPERSEDED.** The invariant as written (Basher walks/classifies/rewires a foreign workflow's params) is the WRONG boundary: Basher modelling ComfyUI's internals. Go-forward = the **two-node contract** (`docs/COMFYUI-BASHER-NODES.md`): `basher_controller` (any input, `kind` spans float/int/string/bool/image/video; AnyType `*` output ‚Äî author DECLARES the control surface by wiring, Basher only enumerates its own `basher_*` nodes) + `basher_export` (any output sink) + one whole-workflow progress bar. Basher NEVER parses the foreign graph. FIRST increment = real control passes (depth/normal/beauty via material overrides into the `PassEncoder` seam) ‚Äî pure WebGL, locally verifiable, previews in the [[V80]] Render Result view. When increments land: add the dharana **Basher ‚Üî ComfyUI** boundary (arm's-length API; observe BOTH sides ‚Äî compiled-JSON snapshot vs `/history` record) + the krama compile lifecycle (ingest‚Üíbind‚Üíbake‚Üíclassify‚Üíinsert-schedule‚Üírewire‚Üísubmit‚Üícollect‚Üístitch).

## V82 ‚Äî Control passes (depth/normal/beauty) render REAL geometry pixels on the ONE production render core via a scene-wide material OVERRIDE ‚Äî no parallel scene walk; depth = content-normalized linear eye-depth, normal = view-space (n+1)/2; eyeballable in the [[V80]] Render Result view [PARTIAL ‚Äî current-frame preview path SHIPPED; `runRenderJob` frame-range batch DEFERRED to Inc 2/3]

**The invariant:** a control pass is NOT a separate renderer and NOT a stub ‚Äî it is the EXISTING `renderSceneToImageCanvas` core (`renderToImage.ts`, the same one #168/#189 beauty use) rendering the LIVE production scene through the production camera with `scene.overrideMaterial` set (the dharana "do not invent a parallel walk ‚Äî SceneFromDAG already exists" rule). Beauty = no override (byte-identical default). Depth/normal render into a RAW target (`NoColorSpace` + `NoToneMapping`) so read-back bytes are the LINEAR values a ControlNet consumes, not display-curved sRGB; the shared chrome hide-pass still excludes editor objects ([[V37]]). Normal = `MeshNormalMaterial` (view-space (n+1)/2 packed RGB). Depth = a custom linear eye-depth shader (`-mvPosition.z`) normalized over the VISIBLE CONTENT's bounding-sphere depth range (`dist(cam,centre) ¬± radius`), inverted so near=white ‚Äî relative/MiDaS-style, NOT frustum-normalized (see [[H119]]). The `pass` selector lives in the [[V80]] Render Result view; the result + its `pass` are parked in `renderResultStore` (ephemeral).

**Breaks when:** a control pass is rendered by rebuilding a three.js scene from `SceneValue` POJOs (a second renderer that drifts from what the viewport shows ‚Äî the parallel-walk trap); depth/normal go through the sRGB/tone-mapped beauty target ‚Üí the encoded values are gamma-distorted and useless to a ControlNet; depth uses `MeshDepthMaterial` (near-black) or frustum-normalization (flat silhouette) instead of content-normalized linear eye-depth ([[H119]]); a pass is asserted "real" from "is it non-blank?" instead of EYEBALLING the PNG (a render that produces an image still produces the WRONG image ‚Äî Lokayata). Type: STRUCTURAL (one render core, override-not-rebuild). Sibling of [[V81]] (the epic this unblocks ‚Äî control passes were its Inc-1 foundation blocker), [[V37]] (chrome-excluded render), [[V80]] (the view that makes eyeballing passes possible), [[H119]] (the two depth traps). REF: `src/render/renderToImage.ts` (`renderViaPass`/`makeLinearDepthMaterial`/`visibleContentSphere`/`depthRange`), `src/app/renderImageAction.ts` (`pass` thread), `src/app/RenderResultView.tsx` (selector), `tests/e2e/p-comfy-inc1-control-passes.spec.ts` (falsifiable). Provenance: ORIGIN = 2026-06-24 ComfyUI Inc 1, user chose "eyeballable foundation first" over the full `runRenderJob` batch wiring ‚Äî so the current-frame preview path is real, the frame-range‚Üístorage batch (for the ComfyUI feed) is deferred to Inc 2/3.

## V83 ‚Äî The video editing surface is ONE After Effects-style layer timeline over the existing DAG; a `Composition` holds ordered `Layer`s, a layer's `source` is ANY time-varying Image producer (MediaClip / scene-render / ComfyWorkflow / nested Composition), a video effect is a typed Image‚ÜíImage operator in the [[V58]] stack, layer props keyframe via [[V57]], and the node-graph view is a DEFERRED projection ‚Äî there is no second pipeline and no separate NLE/dopesheet/compositor [PARTIALLY IMPLEMENTED ‚Äî design doc `docs/COMPOSITOR-DESIGN.md`; spine 1a‚Äì1d SHIPPED: data model + media ingest + Video mode (3rd editor space) + layer Add + layer timeline structure + bar drag (trim/slide/reorder) + twirl-down keyframe rows (opacity + rotation) + the LIVE composite viewer (images, opacity/transform/blend, enabled/solo/trim) + video-mode transport (play/pause/scrub + draggable ruler) + export (MP4/PNG) + the FIRST video effect (Color Correct, Image‚ÜíImage on the V58 stack) + KEYFRAMEABLE effect params (2b ‚Äî Brightness/Contrast/Saturation each a V57-animatable sub-row targeting the effect node, drawn on the track ruler; animated grade shows in viewer+export for free via the H40 read path) + KEYFRAMEABLE Vec2 layer props (3c-ii ‚Äî Position/Scale, two axis fields + one diamond keying a `KeyframeChannelVec2`, drawn on the track; animated 2D transform shows in viewer+export via the H40 vec2 overlay) + a ComfyUIWorkflow GENERATOR layer source (inc 3 ‚Äî the polymorphic Image source; the node carries an imported `ComfyGraph` (design ¬ß6.2 EVOLVE) seeded with a built-in SD1.5 starter, and KEYFRAME-ANY-PARAM works: a free-floating step-interp `KeyframeChannelText`/`KeyframeChannelImage` bound to `comfy:<nodeId>.<inputName>` drives the decoded STUB frame across a scrub via the H40 `resolveEvaluatedParam` read; the pure ComfyGraph compiler core ‚Äî `importComfyGraph` manifest + `compilePreviewFrame` ¬ß7.2 ‚Äî is the snapshot-tested GPU-free IP. Real ComfyUI `/prompt` submit + inspector authoring rows (H104) = next slices). Video decode (1b.2) SHIPPED 2026-06-26 ‚Äî MP4/WebM VIDEO layers decode end-to-end via an HTMLVideoElement path in `WebCodecsMediaDecode` (blob-URL load ‚Üí metadata probe ‚Üí seek-to-time + `createImageBitmap` per frame; per-source element cache + serialized seeks; codec-agnostic ‚Äî uses the browser's decoders; KNOWN-LIMIT = fixed 30fps re-sample, native-fps needs a demuxer). Picker accepts `.mp4/.webm/.mov/.m4v`. e2e `p-compositor-video-layer` (image + mp4 layers composite, scrub changes the frame; VP9-in-MP4 fixture for CI codec portability ‚Äî [[H123]]). ALSO fixed [[H122]]: the top MenuBar dropdown (z-40) opened BEHIND the z-45 video-slot ‚Üí dead menus in video mode ‚Üí `z-50` (e2e `p-menubar-video-zindex`).]

**The invariant (target):** the director sees ONE timeline. A `Composition` is a DAG node holding an ordered `Layer` list (index 0 = back, last = front; nesting a comp in a layer = sequencing). A `Layer` wraps a time-varying `Image` `source` with composite params (trim/startFrame/blend/opacity/2D-transform); `opacity` + transform are keyframeable via free-floating [[V57]] channels ‚Äî the twirl-down dopesheet rows. A layer's source is polymorphic on the EXISTING `Image` socket (the [[V78]] "one socket, discriminate on value.kind" discipline one level up): a `MediaClip` (baked video/image), a scene-render of a `Shot` (the earlier Shot-vs-MediaClip fork dissolves ‚Äî both are sources), a `ComfyWorkflow` ([[V81]] ‚Äî the keyframe compiler lands inside a Comfy layer), or a nested `Composition`. A video effect (color/inpaint/extend/edit/first-last-frame) is a typed `Image‚ÜíImage` operator spliced onto the source edge via the SAME `operatorStack.ts` helpers that drive geometry modifiers ([[V58]], Mesh‚ÜíMesh generalized to Image‚ÜíImage; add/remove/reorder/mute = pure re-wire); local effects are shaders, AI effects COMPILE to a ComfyUI graph ([[V81]]) ‚Äî that is "visible in both Basher and ComfyUI". The viewer is the [[V80]] 2D View; export reuses `createMp4Sink`. All evaluators are pure metadata (V2/V3) ‚Äî per-frame decode + pixel composite happen at the viewer/runtime seam (mirrors Scene‚Üírenderer; ImageValue is lazy P4 metadata). The compositor re-evaluates a layer's source at a time-shifted ctx (comp playhead ‚Üí source-local time via startFrame/inPoint) for the actual frame ‚Äî the time-remap is NOT baked in the source evaluator (`mediaClipFrameAt` is the ONE shared mapping, no drift ‚Äî H40).

**Breaks when:** a separate NLE / dopesheet / compositor surface is built instead of the ONE layer timeline (the three-surfaces trap the whole design exists to avoid); a video effect is built as a one-off instead of a typed operator on the [[V58]] stack (the chain wiring/UI/serialize/mute duplicated ‚Äî the same trap V58 catalogues for constraints/modifiers); a second keyframe road is introduced for layer props instead of reusing the [[V57]] channels; a parallel scene-walk renders a scene layer instead of the ONE production render core ([[V82]]/[[V37]]); a node-graph UI is built NOW as a peer rather than deferred (it's a free future projection of the same DAG ‚Äî V34); a layer's source is given a new per-source socket type instead of the polymorphic `Image` socket (the [[V78]] rule loosens); the comp-time‚Üísource-frame remap is duplicated (one in the evaluator, one in the compositor) ‚Üí preview/composite drift. Type: STRUCTURAL (one surface, one substrate, one operator pattern, one keyframe road). Sibling of [[V34]] (one substrate ‚Äî the node view is a projection), [[V57]] (layer-prop + comfy keyframes), [[V58]] (effects = operators), [[V78]] (one source socket, discriminate on kind), [[V80]] (the viewer), [[V81]] (ComfyUI layer + AI-effect compile), [[V82]] (scene-render passes).

**Status:** NOT YET IMPLEMENTED (spine-first; epic #235, spine #236). **Spine 1a SHIPPED** (`56af9b5`, 2026-06-24) ‚Äî the data model: pure `Composition` / `Layer` / `MediaClip` DAG nodes + values, new `Composition`+`Layer` socket types, `mediaClipFrameAt` shared time‚Üíframe mapping, 7 pure-evaluator unit tests (V2 value-identity + forwarding). **Spine 1b SHIPPED** (`88211d4`) ‚Äî the `MediaDecodeCapability` V6 boundary (`StubMediaDecode` deterministic + `WebCodecsMediaDecode` real IMAGE decode via createImageBitmap + `pickMediaDecode`) + `importMediaClipFromFile` (probe‚Üí`ingestSingleFile`‚ÜíOPFS‚ÜíMediaClip node, V34 one ingest path) + File ‚ñ∏ Import Media; VIDEO decode deferred to **1b.2** (MP4 demux + WebCodecs `VideoDecoder` ‚Äî throws a surfaced error until then); 6 unit + a LIVE e2e (real PNG ‚Üí createImageBitmap true dims ‚Üí OPFS ‚Üí MediaClip). Gate tsc0/eslint0/prettier/vitest **1988**. Design ‚Äî `docs/COMPOSITOR-DESIGN.md` (¬ß4 data model, ¬ß5 effects=operators, ¬ß6 composite, ¬ß8 increments). When the COMPOSITE (1d) lands: add a dharana **Composition ‚Üî compositing engine** boundary (silent-failure modes: layer order vs z-order, trim/startFrame off-by-one, blend parity viewer-vs-export, effect mute not bypassing) + the krama composite lifecycle (evaluate source ‚Üí effect chain ‚Üí trim/position ‚Üí transform/opacity/blend ‚Üí accumulate bottom‚Üítop).
