Known-limits: effect-track diamonds READ-ONLY (drag-retime deferred, same as layer props); `gradedCache` grows one entry per distinct (frame, grade) under animation (no eviction ‚Äî amplified by 2b but bounded by ‚â§durationFrames √ó distinct grades); `openEffects` retains a stale id if an open effect is removed (harmless ‚Äî no sub-rows enumerate). NEXT = 1c.3c-ii Vec2 prop rows ¬∑ 1b.2 video decode ¬∑ inc 3 ComfyUI layer ¬∑ agent effect mutator. **Spine 1c.3c-ii ‚Äî KEYFRAMEABLE Vec2 layer props SHIPPED** (Slice A `e18dc8e` infra + Slice B `15497ca` UI) ‚Äî Position + Scale keyframe in the layer twirl-down. **Slice A:** a new `KeyframeChannelVec2` node (the 2-component sibling of `KeyframeChannelVec3` ‚Äî same function-of-time `sample(seconds)` shape, shared `sampleVec2Keyframes` interp core in `keyframeInterp.ts`, default cubic), the `Vec2` value type + union member, registration, and the keying-path wiring: `inferValueType` (length-2 ‚Üí 'vec2'), `channelNodeFor`, the native first-key allowed list, `keyframe` mutator `VALUE_SHAPE_BY_TYPE`/`DEFAULT_EASING_BY_TYPE` (without the mutator entry the SECOND key was silently rejected ‚Äî found by observation, the 2nd-key-missing pixel test, not unit tests), `overlayChannels.blend` vec2 lerp. **Slice B:** `useAnimatableVec2Field` (the vec2 sibling of `useAnimatableField` ‚Äî reads the evaluated vec2 via the SAME `resolveEvaluatedParam`, routes the single-write edit, keys the whole vector); `LayerTimeline` Position/Scale rows = TWO axis fields + ONE `ParamDiamond` keying the whole vector (NPanel VectorField shape); `collectCompositeInputs` now OVERLAYS `transform.position`/`transform.scale` via `resolveEvaluatedParam` (vec2) ‚Äî `drawComposite` already applied them, so an animated 2D transform shows in viewer+export FOR FREE (H40). OBSERVED (pixel-proven, p-compositor-vec2-keyframe √ó3): a 2-key Scale animation (x 1‚Üí0.3) squeezes the red region across a scrub (mean < base¬∑0.6); Position channel = `KeyframeChannelVec2`, diamond on-key, track keyframe; one-axis edit writes the whole [x,y]. Gate tsc0/eslint0/prettier/vitest **2044** (+8 vec2 channel unit tests); 29 compositor e2e. Known-limits: `useAnimatableVec2Field.effective` does NOT subscribe to the transient store (matches the scalar hook) ‚Üí editing BOTH axes of an ALREADY-animated param paused-with-autokey-off before keying loses the first axis (the un-animated, single-axis, and autokey-on paths all work); the agent `addChannel` mutator still lacks vec2 (UI keying via `dispatchDirectFirstKey` only); `vec2` reader duplicated in videoLayers + compositeDecode (3-line pure helper, matches the `num` pattern). **Inc 3 (compositor) ‚Äî ComfyUIWorkflow GENERATOR layer source, spine SHIPPED** (`40a90d7`; user chose spine-first stub over real-submit/keyframe-first). The Layer source polymorphism (V83/V78) gains a 2nd kind: the EXISTING `ComfyUIWorkflow` node (it already outputs the Image socket) is now addable via "+ Add Layer ‚ñæ ‚Üí ComfyUI Workflow" (`addComfyWorkflowLayer` ‚Äî ComfyUIWorkflow node + Layer in ONE atomic, a still with out-point = comp duration). `compositeDecode` gains a `kind:'comfy'` source branch: `collectCompositeInputs` builds `CompositeSource{kind:'comfy', path:'comfy:<nodeId>', dims}` and `ensureBitmap`‚Üí`decodeComfyStub` renders a DETERMINISTIC stub frame (solid colour from the node-id hash + a "ComfyUI" label) ‚Äî CI-safe, NO server. All layer affordances (opacity/rotation/position/scale keyframes + Color Correct effects) work on a comfy layer for free (it's just another Image source). OBSERVED: Add ‚Üí "1 layer", composite shows a distinct non-black non-uniform stub, DAG wires ComfyUIWorkflow.out‚ÜíLayer.source. Gate vitest **2044**; 30 compositor e2e (+p-compositor-comfy-layer). **KEY OPEN QUESTION (next slice):** the reused `ComfyUIWorkflow` node is the v0.5 PRESET-based stylization node (`presetId`, RenderJob-oriented), NOT the V81 keyframe-compiler `ComfyGraph` (import-any-workflow API-JSON + param manifest) ‚Äî the real-submit/keyframe-any-param slice must decide: EVOLVE this node to carry a `workflowJson` + manifest, or introduce a distinct node. **CARRY-IN:** the stub cache key `comfy:<nodeId>` does NOT fold params ‚Üí won't re-render on a seed/prompt change; the real-submit slice must key the decode on the node's EVALUATED sourceHash (params + bound channels). NEXT = inc 3 real submit (/prompt‚Üí/history‚Üí/view via the SHIPPED pickComfyUI) + ComfyGraph ingest + keyframe-any-param (mirror the KeyframeChannelVec2 add for new KeyframeChannelText/Image) ‚Üí 1b.2 video decode.

## V84 ‚Äî A continuous gesture (drag / scrub / color-picker drag) that writes the DAG must register ONE undo + activity entry, never one per pointer-move. Coalesce EITHER at the store dispatch layer (a `beginInteraction`/`endInteraction` transaction ‚Äî keeps the live per-move writes for render==gizmo, defers the records into one `AtomicGroup`) OR via a local draft committed once on release. The history records COMMITTED ACTIONS, not the intermediate frames of a gesture.

**Status:** COMPLIANT (all known surfaces fixed; 2026-06-30). Store transaction SHIPPED (`b2a3b89`, `src/core/dag/store.ts` ‚Äî `beginInteraction`/`endInteraction` + buffer guards in dispatch/dispatchBatch/dispatchAtomic; 3 unit tests); all 3 gizmos bracketed (`Gizmo.tsx` `startGizmoDrag`/`endGizmoDrag` + SingleGizmo `onDraggingChanged`). `LightStudioPanel` puck drag bracketed (`ca3d58a`, #238 ‚Äî `onPuckDown`‚Üíbegin, `onPuckUp`‚Üíend, e2e in `p206-light-studio-panel.spec.ts`). Color-picker drags bracketed via the shared `useColorPickerInteraction` hook (`d21bde1`, #239 ‚Äî `MaterialColorRow` + studio-light color; begin-on-first-onChange / flush-on-blur, e2e in `p06-2-material-editor.spec.ts`). Already-compliant via draft-or-commit-on-release: `EditableCurve`, `dragScrub`, compositor `LayerTimeline` bar + keyframe drags, `TimelineCanvas` keyframe retime.

**ALL AUDIT INSTANCES NOW FIXED (audit 2026-06-30, [[H131]]):** (a) ‚úÖ FIXED `ca3d58a` (#238) ‚Äî `LightStudioPanel` puck drag, was `onPuckMove` dispatching per move with a FALSE "auto-coalesces" comment (the store never auto-merged same-path setParams); bracketed onPuckDown/onPuckUp. (b) ‚úÖ FIXED `d21bde1` (#239) ‚Äî color swatch inputs (`MaterialColorRow` native + glTF lobes; studio-light color). CONFIRMED LIVE before fixing: 6 picker `input` ticks ‚Üí 6 undo entries; the generic inspector renders a hex param as a read-only span (NO picker) so the only `<input type=color>` sites are material lobes + the studio-light color. Fixed by the picker-session bracket (begin on first onChange, flush on blur). The shared hook means a NEW color swatch can't reintroduce the leak by re-copying the false belief ‚Äî wire it through `useColorPickerInteraction`.

**Breaks when:** a new drag/scrub surface dispatches the DAG per move without bracketing (each frame of the gesture becomes a separate Cmd+Z); OR an author ASSUMES the store auto-coalesces consecutive same-path setParams (it does NOT ‚Äî that false belief is the [[H131]] second-order bug). The reusable test: drag the control, count undo entries ‚Äî must be 1. Does NOT apply to gestures that write `timeStore`/UI-selection only (Timebar slider, pan-zoom, box-select). Type: BEHAVIORAL (undo granularity). Sibling of [[V1]] (one dispatch entry seam); enforced by [[H131]].

## V85 ‚Äî Every editor VISUAL of an animatable DAG object must reflect that object's EVALUATED pose/value at the current playhead and follow it PER-FRAME ‚Äî never the static frame-0 channel-blind read. Animatable visual without a live-`seconds` follower = it freezes at frame 0 while the gizmo + real object move (the render-source split).

**The invariant:** `SceneFromDAG` evaluates the React tree at a FROZEN `ctx.time=0` (P7.10); animation reaches the viewport through per-frame `useFrame` overlays that re-sample the EVALUATED value at `useTimeStore.getState().seconds` and mutate the live three.js object (`DirectChannelsR` meshes, `DirectChannelsLightR` lights, `SceneEnvChannelsR` env, `EditorViewCamera`‚Üí`resolveActiveCameraPoseAt` for the look-through camera). THEREFORE any visual that represents an animatable object MUST be on a follower of the same shape: a channel-evaluated pose/value resolver at `seconds`, re-applied each frame. Two failure modes, BOTH must be avoided: (1) the visual's pose resolver is channel-BLIND (reads raw params, ignores `KeyframeChannel*` ‚Äî e.g. `resolveCameraFrustumPose`), so a keyframed/gizmo-channel edit never reaches it; (2) the visual has no `useFrame` follower, so even a channel-aware value wouldn't track during smooth playback (a prop change only updates on React re-render). The static frame-0 channel-blind read is valid ONLY for non-animatable chrome (grid, fixed editor fill lights).

**Status:** COMPLIANT for all animatable object visuals (2026-07-01, `7515dfb`). Followers: meshes (`DirectChannelsR`), lights (`DirectChannelsLightR`), scene env (`SceneEnvChannelsR`), look-through camera (`EditorViewCamera`), AND now ‚Äî via the shared `usePlayheadFollow` hook ‚Äî the camera frustum (`CameraFrustumFollower` over the new `resolveCameraPoseAt`, #240) and light wireframe helpers (`LightHelperFollower`, #241, scene + rig). Each editor-helper follower mounts only when the object is animated (parity with `DirectChannelsR`'s gate). N/A: `EditorLights` (fixed fill), `DiffOverlay` (transient diff preview). NARROWER GAPS ‚Äî see [[H132]] for the actionable detail: **GAP 1 ‚úÖ FIXED (#242, 2026-07-01)** ‚Äî diagnosis showed MESHES already follow an animated ancestor Group (the Group's `DirectChannelsR` re-renders its subtree) and a grouped LIGHT loses its separate helper entirely (cross-socket reparent out of `scene.lights`), so the gap reduced to the **camera frustum only** (the narrow fix): widen the frustum mount gate to "has an animated ancestor" (`animatedAncestorSet`) ‚Äî `resolveCameraPoseAt` already composes the ancestor world at live `seconds`. **GAP 2 ‚úÖ FIXED (#243, 2026-07-01)** ‚Äî a Track-To'd AreaLight's helper aim froze (the channel-only follower never re-resolved the derived aim) while the lit RectAreaLight followed via `useAreaLightAim`; fix = widen the gate to mount the follower for a constrained AreaLight + re-resolve `resolveTrackToTarget` at `seconds` into `value.lookAt` (the value-recompute analogue of `resolveCameraPoseAt`'s camera Track-To overlay). BOTH narrower gaps now CLOSED ‚Äî V85 is fully COMPLIANT incl. animated-ancestor + constrained-aim helper following.

**Breaks when:** a new editor helper/visual for an animatable object is fed `SceneFromDAG`'s frame-0 evaluate (or a channel-blind raw-param resolver) without a per-frame follower ‚Üí it desyncs from the gizmo (which seeds from the EVALUATED pose at current `seconds`) and from the real rendered object the moment the object is animated and the playhead leaves frame 0. The reusable test: animate the object, scrub to a frame > 0, assert the helper's live world pose == the object's evaluated pose at that frame (boundary-pair); and drag the gizmo, assert the helper tracks. Type: DATA-FLOW + STRUCTURAL (one render-source per object; visual==gizmo==render at the current playhead). Sibling of [[V37]] (viewport==render parity), [[V56]] (`resolveActiveCameraPoseAt` the evaluated camera pose), [[H40]] (the evaluator-vs-surface read-side boundary); enforced by [[H132]].

## V86 ‚Äî The camera lookAt is a SINGLE resolved datum (`resolveCameraPoseAt` ‚Üí `pose.lookAt`, which overlays keyframe channels AND the Track-To constraint), and EVERY lookAt consumer derives from that one resolver ‚Äî never the raw `lookAt` param. The aim is polymorphic on ONE axis (a free authored point OR a Track-To'd object's world position) with NO consumer branching: bind the target in one place (a `TrackTo` node) and the look-through camera, the editor reticle, and the DoF focus distance all follow for free [IMPLEMENTED ‚Äî #247]

**The invariant:** a Basher camera aims via a POINT (`lookAt`), and that point has ONE authoritative resolution ‚Äî `resolveCameraPoseAt(state, cameraId, seconds)` (activeCamera.ts), which composes: raw param ‚Üí keyframe-channel overlay ‚Üí Track-To constraint override (`resolveTrackToTarget`, [[V60]]) ‚Üí parent world. Consumers MUST read `pose.lookAt`, not `node.params.lookAt`: (1) the look-through/production camera (`resolveActiveCameraPoseAt` ‚Üí `EditorViewCamera`, still/anim render); (2) the editor **reticle** (`CameraGizmo` seeds `aimNode` from the pose each playhead change, so a bound reticle sits on its target and follows on scrub/playback; #247); (3) the **DoF focus distance** when `focusOnTarget` (|position ‚àí lookAt| from the pose, fed to `resolveCameraDof` at the viewport `SceneFromDAG` + still `renderImageAction` sites; #247). Because the aim is resolved once, "attach the lookAt to any object" is a ONE-NODE operation (add/point a `TrackTo` with `aimNode=<object>`, `target=<camera>`) that every consumer honours with zero per-consumer wiring.

**Status:** COMPLIANT (2026-07-02, #247). The reticle reads the pose (blue + read-only when `constraintTargetSet` includes the camera); the inspector "look at target" picker (`CameraLookAtTarget`) is the ONE write site for the binding; DoF focus derives from the same pose. e2e: `p248-camera-lookat-target` (bind ‚Üí look-through + reticle both on target; follows a moved target; clear freezes the aim), `p249-camera-dof-focus-on-target` (focus = |cam‚àílookAt|, follows the bound target).

**Breaks when:** a new consumer of the camera aim (a new helper, an export path, an agent tool, a physics/focus system) reads the raw `lookAt` param instead of `resolveCameraPoseAt(...).lookAt` ‚Üí it ignores a Track-To binding (and keyframe channels) and desyncs from the look-through camera the moment the camera tracks a target or is animated. The tell: "I set a look-at target and the render aims at it, but [my new thing] still points at the old authored lookAt." Type: DATA-FLOW + STRUCTURAL (single-source aim). Sibling of [[V77]] (the lookAt+roll ‚Üî orientation bijection every consumer derives from), [[V60]] (the Track-To scene-layer constraint), [[V85]] (per-frame follower of the evaluated pose), [[V51]] (lens+DoF pure mappings, viewport==render). Enforced by [[H134]] (the reticle is a distinct target glyph, not a 2nd gizmo).

### V42 ‚Äî A user-facing alert/overlay must render ABOVE every chrome surface it overlaps, so its controls stay interactable; "visible" is not "reachable"

**Invariant:** any surface that spans a region also occupied by other chrome (a full-width top banner over the floating side panels, a toast, a modal) MUST have a z-index strictly greater than the chrome it overlaps ‚Äî an error/alert is the top of the interaction stack (below only toasts). Equal z-index resolves by DOM order, which is incidental, so an overlay at the SAME z-index as a panel it overlaps is silently occluded: it renders (looks fine) but its controls hit-test to the panel on top. "Element is visible" (getByTestId/toBeVisible) does NOT imply "element is reachable" (a click lands on it) ‚Äî the two diverge exactly at an occlusion boundary.

**Why it matters:** the failure is invisible to the eye (the banner shows) and to naive existence checks (the testid resolves), so it ships. It only surfaces as a user who can't click the control, or a Playwright actionability timeout ("visible, enabled and stable" never satisfied). The z-scale must be a deliberate ladder, not per-component guesses: Basher's is side islands 20 (desktop) / 40 (narrow) < error banner 50 < toasts 100. A new full-region overlay that picks a z-index by copying a neighbour re-opens this class.

**Status:** IMPLEMENTED 2026-07-03 (#261, [[H141]]) for the asset-error banner (was zIndex 20, tied with the inspector island ‚Üí Dismiss occluded; raised to 50). NOT YET generalized: no lint/test asserts the z-ladder ordering, so a future overlay can still pick a colliding z-index. Detection is the elementFromPoint-at-control-centre probe (returns a different element ‚áí occluded).

**Enforcement:** `tests/e2e/p83-asset-error-boundary.spec.ts` (P83#2 ‚Äî clicks Dismiss; a regression re-occludes and the click times out at 30s). REF: `src/app/AssetErrorBanner.tsx` (zIndex 50), `src/app/Layout.tsx` (side-island z 20/40), `src/app/ToastViewport.tsx` (z-[100]). Cross-ref [[H141]], [[H103]] (the "Playwright green while the human can't reach it" family). Branch `ux-overhall`.

### V43 ‚Äî An asset is "available" only when its bytes are READABLE and non-empty, never on mere existence; and a first-boot seeder is idempotent on CONTENT, not on the path existing

**Invariant:** two coupled rules for OPFS-seeded catalog assets. (1) The seeder (`seedAssetsIntoStorage`) may skip an entry ONLY if the existing file is non-empty ‚Äî a 0-byte entry (a prior seed interrupted mid-write: OPFS cleared, tab killed, quota hiccup) must be treated as unseeded and re-fetched. An `exists`-only skip strands the empty file permanently. (2) "Availability" surfaced to the user (Library draggable state) means readable-and-non-empty, not `storage.exists` ‚Äî existence is true for a 0-byte file AND momentarily true mid-rewrite.

**Why it matters:** the two gaps compose into a silent trap: a stranded 0-byte file is `exists=true` ‚Üí Library marks it available ‚Üí the user drags it ‚Üí the importer reads empty bytes ‚Üí `parseGltfJson: not valid JSON`. The asset LOOKS present everywhere except at the one moment it's read. Deterministic, not flaky (the empty file persists). Any consumer that gates on existence rather than content inherits this ‚Äî the fix belongs at the seeder (content-idempotent) AND every availability/read site (wait for non-empty).

**Status:** PARTIAL 2026-07-03 (#262, [[H142]]). DONE: seeder is content-idempotent (`read().byteLength > 0` skip, else re-fetch); the P1#1b e2e waits for readable bytes before dropping. NOT YET: `AssetLibrary` availability is still `storage.exists` (not size) ‚Äî the momentary-mid-rewrite window remains, mitigated only by the seeder now producing non-empty files. A full fix makes availability mean exists-AND-non-empty.

**Enforcement:** `src/app/asset/seedOpfs.test.ts` (re-seeds a 0-byte entry; skips one with content ‚Äî no redundant fetch; falsified: exists-only skip ‚Üí red). `tests/e2e/p1-acceptance.spec.ts` (P1#1b real drag-drop reads readable bytes). REF: `src/app/asset/seedOpfs.ts`, `src/app/AssetLibrary.tsx` (availability = exists ‚Äî the residual gap). Cross-ref [[H142]]. Branch `ux-overhall`.

### V44 ‚Äî Every UI action gated on a selection/mode state must have a production USER GESTURE that sets that state; a gate without a reachable setter is a dead control

**Invariant:** if a control is disabled unless some selection/mode store field is set (`disabled={activeX === null}`), there must exist a real user gesture (click/key/drag) in PRODUCTION code ‚Äî not just a test seam ‚Äî that sets `activeX` for the common case. The gate and the gesture are a pair: shipping one without the other yields a control that paints but can never enable. Verify reachability by driving the real gesture and reading the store, never by setting the store directly in the test.

**Why it matters:** gate-without-gesture is invisible to existence checks (the button renders), to unit tests (they set the store), and to seam-driven e2e (they bypass the gesture). It only surfaces as a user staring at a live-looking button that won't enable. It arises most often when a surface is rewritten and the old element's handler isn't ported ([[H143]] ‚Äî SVG‚Üícanvas dropped the row `onClick`), or when a toolbar op is added ahead of its selection affordance. The reachability check belongs in the SAME increment as the gated control.

**Status:** IMPLEMENTED 2026-07-03 (#264, [[H143]]) for the dopesheet channel ops ‚Äî canvas row-click now sets `activeChannelId`, arming Key/Simplify/Clear/Mute together. NOT YET generalized: no lint asserts "every `disabled={activeX===null}` has a setter gesture," so a future gated toolbar button can re-open the class.

**Enforcement:** `tests/e2e/p263-channel-mute.spec.ts` drives the REAL row-click (not the seam), then asserts the toolbar arms + Mute silences the render end-to-end. REF: `src/timeline/TimelineCanvas.tsx` (onPointerDown row-select), `src/timeline/TimelineDrawer.tsx` (the gated toolbar). Cross-ref [[H143]]. Branch `ux-overhall`.

### V45 ‚Äî A Track-To/aim constraint resolves in WORLD space but must be re-expressed in the constrained node's PARENT-LOCAL space, and it must drive EVERY aimable light kind, not just AreaLight [IMPLEMENTED ‚Äî #265 (aimable lights) + #266/#267 (nested mount + parent-local); nested READ-side is a follow-up]

**Invariant:** two coupled rules for aim/Track-To constraints ([[V60]]). (1) `resolveConstraintRotation` derives the aim from world positions (origin‚Üítarget via `resolveWorldTransform`, #202), yielding a WORLD rotation ‚Äî but the value it writes is a node's LOCAL rotation param, which equals world rotation ONLY when the parent is identity (the top-level SceneChildNode wrapper). Under a non-identity parent Group the correct value is `parentWorld‚Åª¬π ¬∑ aimWorld` (the world aim expressed in parent-local space); returning the raw world aim points the object wrong by exactly the parent's rotation. (2) The constraint must drive every light kind that HAS a direction ‚Äî DirectionalLight and SpotLight, plus the AreaLight/studio rig ‚Äî not only AreaLight. The `SceneFromDAG` light switch passes `constrained`/`nodeId` to `AreaLightR` alone, so a Track-To'd spot or sun silently ignores its target.

**Why it matters:** both gaps are silent ‚Äî the object renders, just aimed wrong, no error. #1 surfaces the moment any camera/light under a moved/rotated Group is Track-To'd (increasingly common post-#231 groupable lights + cameras). #2 makes "aim this spotlight at the subject" a no-op. The world-transform machinery (#202) already exists; the fix is the parent-local re-expression + widening the light consumer set.

**GROUNDED CORRECTION (Houdini, 2026-07-04) ‚Äî #1 was mis-modelled; the real root cause is a two-graph conflation, not a math tweak.** Live observation + Houdini grounding (`ref/GROUND_TRUTH_HOUDINI_OPERATORS.md` ¬ß0) revealed: the Track-To‚Üírotation overlay (`ConstrainedR`) mounts ONLY at the top-level scene-children loop (`SceneChildNode`); a mesh nested under a Group/Transform renders through the id-less `MeshChild`, which has NO constraint branch ‚Äî so a nested Track-To is a total NO-OP, not "off by the parent's rotation" (the same [[H132]]/#231-Inc-2 nested-node known-limit that also drops nested direct-CHANNELS [[V57]]). Top-level nodes have an identity parent ‚áí the world-as-local math is ALREADY correct there, so `parentWorld‚Åª¬π¬∑aimWorld` alone is unobservable in the render. Houdini names the category: an operator relationship is **edge-less in the value-flow/wire graph** but **edge-ful in the dependency/cook graph** ‚Äî two graphs over the same nodes. Basher's bug is resolving an overlay by WALKING THE RENDER TREE (a value-flow/display structure that drops node-ids at nesting boundaries) instead of by LOOKUP against a flat id namespace + a synthesized dependency edge (Houdini's Export Constraints CHOP reaches "any object regardless of its position in the hierarchy‚Ä¶ bypassing traditional parenting"; `addExtraInput()` re-registers the dep edge every cook). "Thread ids through GroupR/TransformR" was the WRONG instinct ‚Äî the fix is structural: (B1) a flat `id‚Üínode` map populated at every depth, (B2) a synthesized `overlay‚Üítarget` dep edge so the nested target recooks, (B3) name the two graphs. That fix makes nested constraints AND nested channels work uniformly at any depth. Cameras/lights aim by a WORLD point (lookAt/`.target`), parent-invariant, so they DON'T have the parent-local problem ‚Äî #2 is fully independent and reachable NOW.

**Status:** PARTIAL ‚Äî split into independent tracks. **#2 (I4/C7, aimable-light consumer set) = IMPLEMENTED (#265, `ux-overhall`).** A top-level SpotLight/DirectionalLight now obeys a Track-To: `LightKindR` forwards `constrained`/`nodeId` to `DirectionalLightR` + `SpotLightR` (not just AreaLightR), and a shared `useLightTargetAim` hook (the `.target`-based analogue of `useAreaLightAim`'s `.lookAt`) writes `resolveTrackToTarget` ‚Üí `light.target.position` per frame; the authored-target `useEffect` is gated `if (constrained) return` so the two don't fight. `isAimableLightKind` (Area/Spot/Directional) is ONE predicate shared by the render mount gate AND `LightHelperFollower` (widened via `aimLightValueForHelper` ‚Äî lookAt/target/rotation per kind) so render==helper can't drift. OBSERVED live: the spot at `[5,5,0]` went from authored `[0,0,-1]` ‚Üí Track-To `[-0.707,-0.707,0]` (aim at origin). e2e `p265-aimable-light-track-to.spec.ts` (both kinds == normalize(aim‚àípos); mute ‚Üí reverts to authored). **#1 (I2/C5, parent-local) = IMPLEMENTED (#266/#267).** The nested-overlay render mount (B1‚ÄìB3, see [[V88]]) makes a nested `ConstrainedR` mount; `resolveConstraintRotation` re-expresses `parentWorld‚Åª¬π¬∑aimWorld` via the existing `resolveParentWorldMatrix` (null ‚Üí identity ‚Üí byte-identical for a top-level node, so p204 stays green). OBSERVED: a box under a Y-90¬∞ Transform + Track-To ‚Üí rendered ‚àíZ aims at the target (would be off by the parent's 90¬∞ without the re-express); `p266-nested-overlay.spec.ts`. KNOWN-LIMIT: the READ side (`resolveEvaluatedTransform`) still resolves only top-level nodes, so a nested constrained node's gizmo/inspector don't show the aim (render is correct) ‚Äî a follow-up, and nested native-mesh selection isn't wired either.

**Enforcement:** #2 ‚Äî e2e per aimable light kind: Track-To a top-level Directional/Spot at a target, assert `__basher_light_world_aims` direction == normalize(target‚àíposition) (render==intended); falsify by muting ‚Üí reverts to authored target. #1 ‚Äî e2e that Track-To's an object under a NON-IDENTITY parent Group and asserts rendered `-Z` (`__basher_mesh_world_quaternion`) points at the target ‚Äî REQUIRES B1‚ÄìB3 first (a bare parent-local math change stays render-invisible; the current falsification is that a nested constraint renders nothing). REF: `ref/GROUND_TRUTH_HOUDINI_OPERATORS.md` (¬ß0 two-graph, ¬ß4 constraint invariants I1‚ÄìI12, ¬ß5 delta backlog A1/A2/B1‚ÄìB3), `src/app/nodeConstraints.ts` (`resolveConstraintRotation`), `src/app/resolveTrackTo.ts`, `src/app/resolveWorldTransform.ts` (#202), `src/viewport/SceneFromDAG.tsx` (light switch + `MeshChild` render bypass). Cross-ref [[V60]] (edge-less scene-layer constraint), [[V57]] (nested channels share the B1‚ÄìB3 fix), [[V87]]/[[V88]] (the full SOP/CHOP invariant sets this is one row of). Branch `ux-overhall`.

### V87 ‚Äî The SOP (edge-WIRED geometry-operator) invariant set: a modifier is a value-flow node that composes at any depth for free, but must uphold determinism, handle-not-buffers, type-directed attribute transform, and role-typed arity [PARTIAL ‚Äî S2/S3/S4(part)/S7/S8 IMPLEMENTED; S12‚ÄìS21 GAPS]

**The invariant:** a geometry modifier (the SOP half of [[V58]]/[[V64]]) is edge-WIRED (`base mesh ‚Üí mod ‚Üí consumer`); because its output VALUE flows up through nesting, it composes at any depth automatically (unlike an edge-less constraint [[V60]] ‚Äî the contrast that PROVED the sub-chain fits geometry). Grounded end-to-end against Houdini (`ref/GROUND_TRUTH_HOUDINI_OPERATORS.md` ¬ß2, `ref/houdini/SOP.md`, 16 SideFX URLs). The full class set: **S1** value-flow closure (out-type==in-type, stackable); **S2** handle-not-buffers (rebuildable `GeometryRef`, never inline arrays ‚Äî Houdini packed-prim reference model ‚úì); **S3** deterministic rebuild-from-params ‚úì; **S4** clone-don't-mutate cached source ([[H111]]) + reverse winding on negative determinant ([[H112]], Reverse SOP ‚úì); **S5** one projection two roads (render==read descriptor key); **S6** ordered stack, one wiring authority (OperatorStack), reorder=splice; **S7** mute=identity passthrough at evaluate (Houdini bypass ‚úì); **S8** local-space authoring / world transform inherited above the stack, never baked into a local param ‚úì (but LIVE-VIOLATED by Track-To, see [[V45]]); **S9** derived surfaces (bounds/raycast/UV) read from the BUILT geometry; **S10** params are ordinary animatable channels ([[V57]]); **S11** defined degenerate/async-source passthrough (never blank).

**GAPS Houdini surfaced (ranked for a video tool):** **S12** explicit time-dependence / static-cache flag (HIGHEST ‚Äî Basher scrubs constantly; Houdini caches non-time-dependent subgraphs across frames; without it every static modifier rebuilds per frame or a live one goes stale); **S13** type-directed attribute transform incl. **inverse-transpose normals** (S4 covers winding only; first bend/taper/mirror/non-uniform-scale breaks lighting on camera); **S14** four attribute classes, vertex-class ‚âÝ point-class (UV seams / hard edges REQUIRE per-corner attributes; point-only can't represent them; Array already rebuilds geometry); **S15** role-typed N-ary inputs (copy-to-points/boolean/attribute-transfer are binary/n-ary with role-typed inputs ‚Äî design the arity model now); **S16** component-group selection scoping; **S17** topology-change invalidation + attribute interpolation onto new components (extends S9); **S18** lazy dirty-driven recook; **S19** node error/warning surfacing (extends S11); **S20** lock/freeze snapshot; **S21** attribute promotion between classes (needs S14).

**Breaks when:** a modifier inlines buffers (S2 ‚Üí [[V43]] cost leak); the two roads build the descriptor key differently (S5 ‚Üí [[H40]] render‚âÝresolver); a transform applies one matrix to all vectors (S13 ‚Üí normals wrong under non-uniform scale, velocity/orient corrupted); a rebuild reads/keys per frame when static (S12 ‚Üí scrub churn) or caches when animated (stale); the substrate stays unary when the next node is copy-to-points (S15 ‚Üí re-architect the edge model). Type: STRUCTURAL+DATA-FLOW (the edge-wired operator contract). Sibling of [[V64]] (the modifier substrate this generalizes), [[V58]] (the substrate), [[V88]] (the edge-less CHOP counterpart ‚Äî the two halves), [[V57]] (animatable params), [[V43]] (handle cost class), [[H40]]/[[V37]] (render==resolver). **REF:** `ref/GROUND_TRUTH_HOUDINI_OPERATORS.md` ¬ß2 + ¬ß5.C/E; `ref/houdini/SOP.md` (per-invariant SideFX URLs). Reference-model grounding (Houdini closed-source), not a source trace. Branch `ux-overhall`.

### V88 ‚Äî The CHOP (edge-LESS id-keyed overlay) invariant set: constraints + channels resolve by flat-id lookup + a synthesized dependency edge (never a render-tree walk), are pure over an explicit interval+seed, and layer by weighted order [PARTIAL ‚Äî C2/C3/C6/C8/C10 + N6/N2 IMPLEMENTED (#266); D1 IMPLEMENTED (number/vec2/vec3 extend + cycle + interp modes + handle types #269‚Äì#273); F-MODIFIER STACK IMPLEMENTED (#274, procedural per-channel modifiers ‚Äî Noise; #275, Cycles modifier ‚Äî the D1 cycle family migrated to a first-class stack entry; #276, value-phase Generator + Limits(Y-clamp); #277, time-phase Stepped + Limits(X-clamp) via shared resolveSampleTime; #278, Envelope value-phase reference-band remap ‚Äî the value-phase F-Modifier set is COMPLETE; #279, restricted-range UI ‚Äî the NPanel authoring surface for the modifiers' useRange window + blend-in/out ramps, closing the last authoring gap on the whole F-Modifier stack); D2 (weighted multi-source layering / NLA) + D3‚ÄìD8 GAPS]

**The invariant:** an animation channel ([[V57]]) or relationship constraint ([[V60]]) is an edge-LESS overlay ‚Äî NOT in the value-flow wire graph, resolved at the scene layer and applied on BOTH the render and read sides ([[H40]] one band two callers). Grounded end-to-end against Houdini (`ref/GROUND_TRUTH_HOUDINI_OPERATORS.md` ¬ß3, `ref/houdini/CHOP.md` + `CONSTRAINTS.md` + `NETWORK-META.md`). **The keystone (Houdini): an overlay is edge-less in the VALUE-FLOW graph but edge-ful in the DEPENDENCY graph ‚Äî two graphs over the same nodes.** The class set: **C1** edge-less enumeration keyed by target, O(1) membership (B13); **C2** derived every eval, never baked ‚úì; **C3** render overlay == read overlay, same primitive ‚úì ([[H40]]/[[V37]]); **C4** scene-layer resolution, never in a bare evaluate; **C5** world-output re-expressed to the slot's local frame (`parentWorld‚Åª¬π`, see [[V45]] ‚Äî GAP); **C6** cycle-safe: reads un-aimed upstream/self world only ‚úì; **C7** drive every capable target in native form (mesh rotation, camera/light lookAt point ‚Äî mesh+camera+AreaLight+SpotLight+DirectionalLight all obey Track-To as of #265, [[V45]] #2 CLOSED; Point/Ambient are omnidirectional, no aim); **C8** one math core reused by consumers AND tests ‚úì; **C9** pure over an explicit interval [start,t] + seed, no live scene-graph reads (RESTATED ‚Äî see below); **C10** degenerate‚Üíauthored fallback, never blank/throw ‚úì; **C11** time-snapshot sampling, membership-gated mounting ([[H48]]); **C12** defined precedence/coexistence (channels+constraint order); **C13** mute contributes nothing uniformly.

**N6/N2 IMPLEMENTED (#266/#267, `ux-overhall`) ‚Äî the [[V45]] root cause is FIXED.** Overlays now mount at ANY depth, resolved by FLAT-ID LOOKUP, never a render-tree walk. **B1** ‚Äî the render tree threads each nested child's node id via the EXPORTED `childEdges` (the proven value‚Üíid map from `resolveWorldTransform`; no second walk ‚Äî Chesterton); a container renderer (`GroupR`/`TransformR`/`MaterialOverrideR`) renders each child through `RenderChild`, which looks membership up in the flat sets. **B2 (the synthesized dependency edge)** ‚Äî the membership sets live in an `OverlayMembershipContext` MEMOIZED ON A CONTENT SIGNATURE (`overlaySig`); adding an EDGE-LESS overlay to a nested node flips the sig ‚Üí every mounted `RenderChild` re-evaluates membership ‚Üí the target mounts its overlay (finding ‚âÝ dependency ‚Äî without this the nested target, whose parent's evaluated `value` is unchanged by the edge-less overlay, would never re-render). A non-overlay edit keeps the sig stable ‚Üí `RenderChild`s bail (H48/B13 preserved). **B3** ‚Äî the value-flow render tree (`MeshChild`/containers) and the id-keyed overlay resolution (`RenderChild`/`OverlayDispatch`, ONE shared dispatch with the top-level `SceneChildNode`) are separate concerns. ONE fix made nested constraints ([[V60]]) AND nested channels ([[V57]]) work uniformly. Houdini's Export Constraints CHOP reaches "any object regardless of hierarchy position, bypassing parenting" ‚Äî the grounded target. OBSERVED: a box nested under a Y-90¬∞ Transform + Track-To ‚Üí rendered ‚àíZ aims correctly (`p266-nested-overlay.spec.ts`); nested position channel animates its world position; both were total no-ops before. **KNOWN-LIMIT (follow-up):** the READ side (`resolveEvaluatedTransform`, gizmo/inspector) still matches only TOP-LEVEL scene children, so a nested constrained node's inspector/gizmo don't reflect the aim (nested native-mesh selection isn't wired either); the RENDER is correct. Cross-ref [[H144]].

**C9 RESTATED (the purity reframe):** stateful CHOPs (Lag/Spring/Filter) integrate over time ‚Üí output at t depends on history, seemingly contradicting "pure function of (state,time)." Resolution: Houdini's determinism comes from a fixed cook contract (re-derive the interval from a known seed), NOT statelessness. So `spring(seed, input[start..t])` IS pure ‚Äî of the seed+interval, not scalar t. The clause C9 protects (no live scene-graph reads ‚Äî the cycle hazard [[V60]]/C6) survives: a spring reading its own history buffer is a cache it owns, not a live read. ‚áí C9 = "pure over an explicit interval + seed, no live scene reads"; stateful ops (D7) are a sibling class with a mandatory seed + replay-or-cache contract; both C3 roads must share the seed + window.

**GAPS Houdini surfaced (ranked):** **D1** extend/extrapolation conditions per channel (hold/slope/cycle/**cycle-with-offset**/mirror ‚Äî **PARTIAL, #269**: implemented as per-side `extendBefore`/`extendAfter` ‚àà {hold,cycle,cycle-offset,mirror,slope} for the NUMBER/VEC2/VEC3 channels; the domain is the authored keyframe span [first,last]; the rule lives in the sample function (`planExtend` + `sample*KeyframesExtended` in `keyframeInterp.ts`), so ALL callers ‚Äî 3D render, read-side gizmo/inspector, compositor ‚Äî get it via `ch.sample()` (H40, one place). Default `hold` on both sides = byte-identical to the pre-#269 clamp (V49 parity, proven by the full suite). **INSPECTOR AUTHORING SHIPPED (#270, `ux-overhall`):** a per-side "Extend / Before / After" control (`ChannelExtendControls` in `NPanel.tsx`) lives in the channel's ANIMATE section, enumerating the exported `CHANNEL_EXTEND_RULES` via two `<select>`s and wiring through `setParam`. The two params ROUTE to 'animate' in `paramToSection` (leaving the raw-fallback bucket, mirroring how Environment/Camera params route to their custom-control section) and the generic rows for them are filtered so they don't double-render. Blender-vindicated: a single per-side affordance is the right director UX. **CYCLE COUNT SHIPPED (#271, `0967d84`):** per-side `cyclesBefore`/`cyclesAfter` (int, 0=‚àû) on the 3 schemas + `planExtend` ‚Äî past N span-periods the side FREEZES (cycle holds the boundary key, cycle-offset holds last+N¬∑delta, slope clamps dt to N¬∑span, mirror clamps time into the window). Freeze value is continuous with the in-cycle value at the transition. Grounded in Blender `FModifierCycles.count`. Surfaced as a per-side count input in the Extend panel (shown only when the side repeats). **ALL-CONSUMER REACH SHIPPED (#270 items 2+3, `466b6a7`):** `activeCamera` scalar pose (fov/near/far/roll + CameraSelect active) + `EditableCurve` draw now route through the `*Extended` samplers (vec3 pose already did via `buildVec3Sampler`) ‚Äî H40 render==read==curve complete for extend. Gated by `p270-camera-extend.spec.ts` (frustum-pose Side A == evaluated-param Side B, cycle-offset fov‚Üí120, falsify hold‚Üí60).
**STILL DEFERRED (D1):** the Houdini `default` rule (needs a per-channel default-value field, ambiguous under overlay); color/quat/text/image channels (own interp / step ‚Äî stay hold); an EXPLICIT domain override (today = keyframe span); an agent mutator. Gated by `keyframeInterp.test.ts` + `p269-channel-extend.spec.ts` (render==read boundary-pair + falsify hold/cycle/cycle-offset) + `p270-extend-inspector.spec.ts` (UI-dropdown ‚Üí live-render travel + cycle-count freeze) + `p270-camera-extend.spec.ts`.

**PER-KEYFRAME INTERPOLATION MODES SHIPPED (#272, `f7eeb2a`+`4ec10e6`) ‚Äî the biggest visible animation-parity gap CLOSED:** the per-keyframe `easing` enum broadened from {linear,cubic} to add Blender's F-Curve interps ‚Äî `constant` (stepped hold) + the Penner easing equations {sine,quad,quart,quint,expo,circ,back,bounce,elastic} ‚Äî plus an optional `ease` direction {in,out,inout} (default inout). Pure engine in `keyframeInterp.ts` (`easeInShape`/`easeFraction`/`easedValue`/`bounceOut`); each segment fn (scalar/vec2/vec3) routes an equation interp through ONE shared eased fraction, ignoring b√©zier handles (Blender's equation interps aren't handle-driven); `constant` holds the source value then snaps at the key. **Convention = DESTINATION-key-governs** (Basher's existing 'cubic' behaviour), read as "how the curve ARRIVES at this key" ‚Äî no fork, byte-identical for legacy linear/cubic (V49 parity, vitest 2173). Shared `KEYFRAME_INTERPS`/`EASE_DIRS` enums exported. UI = a per-keyframe interp+ease picker in the curve editor for the ACTIVE key (`curve-interp-select`/`curve-ease-select`, ease shown only for equation interps), committing through the keyframes-array chokepoint (H40). Gated by `keyframeInterp.test.ts` (constant-hold + endpoint-exactness + Penner midpoints + vec3 shared-fraction) + `p272-interp.spec.ts` (back-out overshoot render==read) + `p272b-interp-picker.spec.ts` (picker ‚Üí setParam ‚Üí render). **HANDLE TYPES SHIPPED (#273, `0c59dc8`) ‚Äî the interpolation story COMPLETE:** an optional per-keyframe `handleType` ‚àà {auto, auto-clamped, vector, aligned, free} on the 3 schemas + the shared sampler. `auto`/`auto-clamped`/`vector` handles are COMPUTED from neighbours at the ARRAY level (`sampleScalarKeyframes` has the full sorted array), so `segmentScalar` stays neighbour-blind for the fast path ‚Äî grounded on Blender `calchandle_fcurve_intern` (fcurve.cc): tangent `dvec_b/len_b + dvec_a/len_a`, `len = |tvec|¬∑2.5614`, boundary reflection, `correct_bezpart` X-monotonic guard; auto-clamped adds the extremum-flatten + per-neighbour clamp; vector points ‚Öì toward the neighbour; free/aligned use the STORED offset (alignment is an edit-time constraint). **Byte-identity: `handleType` undefined ‚Üí the pre-#273 fast path runs verbatim** (proven by the free==undefined unit test + migrations.test + the full 2181-suite) ‚Äî opt-in only, the default handle feel is NEVER flipped. **vec2/vec3 handle-typed segments sample PER-COMPONENT through the scalar path** (each axis is its own F-curve with its own auto tangent ‚Üí render == read == the per-axis curve display, H40). UI = a per-key handle-type picker (`curve-handle-select`) next to the #272 interp picker; computed handles are DISPLAYED (grab affordance == the played curve, via exported `resolveScalarHandle`); dragging a handle converts the key to `free`. Gated by `keyframeInterp.test.ts` (+8: auto overshoots / auto-clamped flattens at extremum / vector=line / free==undefined byte-parity / equation-ignores-handle / vec3 per-component) + `p273-handle-types.spec.ts` (render==read H40 + picker drives render, auto-vs-auto-clamped falsify, live :5180). **DEFERRED:** aligned opposite-handle co-rotation on drag (drag‚Üífree for now); per-handle (left/right independent) type; text/image/color/quat channels stay legacy.

**F-MODIFIER STACK SHIPPED (#274, `5cb5ebe`) ‚Äî V88 D2, the architectural fork:** a per-channel `modifiers: FChannelModifier[]` (default `[]`) on the 3 schemas + a PURE stack engine in `src/nodes/channelModifiers.ts` (`applyChannelModifiers`), applied AFTER the extended base sample INSIDE `sample*KeyframesExtended` ‚Äî the extended samplers were split into `*ExtendedBase` (the verbatim pre-#274 body) + a thin wrapper that applies modifiers, so empty stack = the base verbatim = **byte-identical** (migrations.test + free/full 2193-suite). ONE place ‚Üí every consumer (render, read gizmo/inspector, curve editor draw, `activeCamera` scalar pose via `channelExtendArgs`) gets it through `ch.sample()` (H40 render==read==curve). First modifier = **Noise**: a DETERMINISTIC fractal value-noise (sine-hash lattice + smoothstep) of `t*scale+phase`, blend {add,subtract,multiply,replace}, strength/offset/depth ‚Äî PURE (no `Math.random`, H48/H49), so the curve editor draws the exact curve that plays. Common fields on every modifier: `muted`, `influence` (0-1 blend of effect over the running value), `useRange`+`rangeStart/End/blendIn/Out` (Blender restricted-range ramps). **vec2/vec3 apply modifiers identically per-component** (one modifier = one function of time, Blender-consistent) so the per-axis curve display matches render. Grounded on Blender `fcurve_modifiers.cc` (`fcm_noise_evaluate`, `evaluate_fmodifiers`). UI = `ChannelModifierControls` in the NPanel animate section (`channel-modifier-add` "+ noise", per-modifier params + influence + mute + remove); `modifiers` routes to 'animate' in `paramToSection` (leaves the raw bucket, filtered so no double-render ‚Äî mirrors extendBefore/After). Gated by `channelModifiers.test.ts` (+12: deterministic/bounded noise, empty=byte-identical, blend modes, influence/range blending, mute, through-the-sampler) + `p274-modifiers.spec.ts` (noise deviates render off the clean curve, render==read H40, mute reverts falsify; NPanel "+ noise" button + fields drive render). **This is Basher's answer to "build a stack not enums".** **CYCLES MIGRATION SHIPPED (#275, `b20894f`):** the D1 cycle family is now a first-class `{type:'cycles'}` stack entry (Blender FModifierCycles) ‚Äî hold/slope stay the per-side `extend{Before,After}` EXTRAPOLATION property (enum narrowed 5‚Üí2), cycle/cycle-offset/mirror + counts move to the Cycles modifier (one entry, both sides). Cycles is a TIME modifier: a pure `resolveExtend()` (keyframeInterp.ts) maps the STORED model (extrapolation + a non-muted Cycles entry, mode‚âÝnone OVERRIDES that side's extrapolation) onto the engine's 5-value rule + counts, which `planExtend` + the samplers consume UNCHANGED ‚Äî `applyChannelModifiers` SKIPS the Cycles entry (it is not a value op). Because the engine is byte-for-byte untouched, every existing extend unit test stays green (the strongest byte-identity proof). Per-node migration v1‚Üív2 on the 3 schemas splits old params ‚Üí new (`migrateExtendParamsToCycles`); a slope/hold+count>0 combo (never UI-authorable, absent in Blender's LINEAR/CONSTANT) drops the count with a `console.warn` (no silent loss, V38). UI: the Extend dropdown is now hold/slope; cycling is authored in the Cycles card of `ChannelModifierControls` (`channel-modifier-add-cycles`, per-side mode selects + counts). **first-wins**: `resolveExtend` honours the FIRST non-muted Cycles entry (a 2nd is inert) ‚Äî mirrors the I11 constraint first-wins. Gated by migrations.test (+8: real v1 cycle-offset project load ‚Üí migrated `sample()` == pre-migration engine value byte-identically; count freeze; hold/slope no-modifier; mixed per-side; noise preserved+prepended; idempotent) + keyframeInterp.test (+5 resolveExtend) + the updated p269/p270-extend-inspector/p270-camera e2e (box travels via the Cycles modifier, render==read H40, count freezes, afterMode=none/remove clamps ‚Äî falsify). **VALUE-PHASE MODIFIERS SHIPPED (#276, `7cd5254`):** the two most-common Blender value-phase F-Modifiers, exact Noise template (union member + `modifierValue` case + defaults + card; engine/architecture UNCHANGED, empty stack byte-identical). **Generator** (Blender FMod_Generator, Expanded Polynomial): `y = c0 + c1¬∑t + c2¬∑t¬≤ + ‚Ä¶` (t in seconds), additive (add to curve) or replace; coefficients array + order stepper. **Limits ‚Äî value(Y) clamp ONLY**: `clamp(value, minY, maxY)`, each bound independently enabled. **The phase split is the real architectural boundary** (grounded on the bundled Blender manual `graph_editor/fcurves/modifiers`): Generator + Limits-Y are VALUE-phase (fit `applyChannelModifiers`); **Stepped ("sample every N frames, hold") + Limits-X (drop curve outside frame range) are TIME-phase** ‚Äî they remap/clamp the sample TIME and are DEFERRED to a time-phase increment that generalizes the Cycles-specific `resolveExtend` into a shared `resolveSampleTime(t, modifiers)`. Limits-X deferral is documented in the type (no silent partial). Gated by channelModifiers.test (+10: generator additive/replace/empty/influence/pure, limits clamp/disabled/soft-clamp/compose-after-generator, through-the-sampler) + `p276-value-modifiers.spec.ts` (generator adds off the clean curve, limits clamps, render==read H40, empty reverts; NPanel +generator/+limits buttons + fields drive render). Add-button testid is per-type `channel-modifier-add-<type>`. **TIME-PHASE MODIFIERS SHIPPED (#277, `ee580b5`):** Stepped + Limits-X, generalizing the Cycles-specific handling into a shared PURE `resolveSampleTime(t, modifiers)` (Blender `evaluate_time_fmodifiers`) composed ALONGSIDE Cycles (which stays in `resolveExtend`/`planExtend`, untouched). `resolveSampleTime` runs the TIME modifiers (Stepped, Limits-X) only, applied ONCE at the sampler entry (`sample*KeyframesExtended`) BEFORE the extended base sample; the remapped time `st` feeds BOTH the base sample AND the value phase ‚Äî **Blender-faithful** (a Stepped above a Noise steps the noise too; Blender's value modifiers evaluate at `devaltime`). Identity when no time modifier is present ‚Üí `st === t` bit-for-bit, so `planExtend` + every existing extend/value test stay byte-identical (37 interp tests + full 2227-suite unchanged = strongest proof). **Stepped** (Blender FMod_Stepped): snap `t ‚Üí offset + floor((t-offset)/step)¬∑step` (hold between steps, stop-motion); `step<=0` identity guard; optional own `useFrameRange`+`frameStart/End` (outside ‚Üí unstepped passthrough). **Limits-X** = the TIME half of the existing Limits modifier (one modifier, BOTH phases): `useMinX/useMaxX/minX/maxX` clamp the sample time ‚Üí the curve holds its boundary value outside (Blender "constant extrapolate outside frame range"); `FModLimits` gained the X fields, `FModStepped` is a new union member ‚Äî both additive/defaulted ‚Üí **NO schema version bump** (existing v2 + empty stack byte-identical). Time phase honours `muted`, IGNORES generic influence/range (Blender; NPanel drops the influence row for the pure-time Stepped, keeps it for Limits whose Y clamp is a value op); `applyChannelModifiers` + `modifierValue` skip Stepped like Cycles. UI: stepped card (step/offset/frame-range) + limits X rows in `ChannelModifierControls`. Gated by channelModifiers.test (+11: resolveSampleTime identity/snap/offset/step-guard/frame-range/mute/limits-X/compose; through-the-sampler stepped-holds / limits-X-extrapolates / stepped-steps-a-noise / falsify) + `p277-time-modifiers.spec.ts` (3 boundary-pairs live on :5180: stepped holds render==read H40, limits-X constant-extrapolates render==read, empty reverts; NPanel +stepped step-field + +limits max-X drive render). **ENVELOPE SHIPPED (#278, `4e08c8e`) ‚Äî the value-phase F-Modifier set COMPLETE:** a value-phase `modifierValue` case (no architecture change, exact Noise/Generator template, empty stack byte-identical automatically). Reshapes a curve by mapping a fixed REFERENCE band `[reference+min, reference+max]` onto a per-time ADJUSTED band `[reference+p.min, reference+p.max]` interpolated from keyed control points; a value keeps its position within the reference band as the band shifts (translate) or widens (scale). **GROUNDED on Blender source** `fcm_envelope_evaluate` (the Blender MCP live-probe was DOWN, so fetched the C source + manual `graph_editor/fcurves/modifiers`): remap is byte-equivalent to `fac = (v‚àí(midval+min))/(max‚àímin); out = bandMin + fac¬∑(bandMax‚àíbandMin)`. Model = `reference` (midval) + global `min`/`max` (OFFSETS to the reference band) + `points:[{time,min,max}]` (per-time OFFSETS to the adjusted band; linear interp between points, held outside). **Decisions:** store point min/max as OFFSETS (matches the UI labels); default **empty points ‚Üí no-op** (Blender `env->data==null ‚Üí return`); `addPoint` seeds an IDENTITY point (offsets = global band ‚Üí no jump); degenerate reference band (`max==min`) ‚Üí no-op guard. `FModEnvelope` new union member; nested `points` array additive/defaulted ‚Üí **NO schema version bump** (existing v2 + empty stack byte-identical). Value op ‚Üí keeps influence/range/mute via the existing `applyChannelModifiers` machinery. UI: `ChannelModifierControls` envelope card (reference/min/max + control-point editor: `channel-modifier-<i>-add-point` + per-point `-point-<k>-{time,min,max}` + remove). Gated by channelModifiers.test (+10 golden values from the source formula: identity-band/shift/interp/scale/hold-outside/no-points/degenerate/influence+mute/pure + through-the-sampler) + `p278-envelope-modifier.spec.ts` (2 boundary-pairs live :5180: envelope shift‚Üí6 & scale‚Üí11 render==read H40, empty reverts; NPanel +envelope/+point/point-max drive render). **RESTRICTED-RANGE UI SHIPPED (#279, `dec14e0`) ‚Äî the F-Modifier stack's authoring surface COMPLETE:** the engine already folded `useRange` + `[rangeStart,rangeEnd]` + `blendIn/Out` ramps into each modifier's effective 0..1 influence (`effectiveInfluence` in `channelModifiers.ts`, unit-tested) but the NPanel cards had NO controls ‚Äî a director could only author a restricted range via agent/JSON. Added a shared range sub-section below the influence row on every VALUE-phase modifier card: a `restrict` (useRange) toggle revealing start/end + blend in/out number fields (testids `channel-modifier-<i>-{useRange,rangeStart,rangeEnd,blendIn,blendOut}`). **PURE UI ‚Äî no engine/schema change** (empty-range path byte-identical, 2237 vitest unchanged). Gated to value-phase only (Cycles/Stepped are pure TIME modifiers, ignore influence/range in `resolveSampleTime` ‚Äî same gate as the influence row). Observed live (`p279-range-ui.spec.ts`): a constant Generator (+10 ‚Üí 15) restricted to [0,4] with blend-in=2 attenuates render to 50% inside the ramp (X=10, render==read H40), stays full past the ramp (X=15), and clearing useRange reverts to full everywhere (falsify). **DEFERRED:** per-axis (independent) vec stacks (today a modifier is identical per-component ‚Üí diagonal jitter; true Blender = independent per-axis F-curves, a real sampler-shape change). Distinct from D2's "weighted multi-source layering" (NLA/action-strips ‚Äî still a gap). **GROUNDED vs Blender ‚Äî `ref/GROUND_TRUTH_BLENDER_FCURVE_EXTEND.md`:** Blender SPLITS the two mechanisms ‚Äî a per-F-Curve `extrapolation` ENUM {CONSTANT=hold, LINEAR=slope} + a STACKABLE `FModifierCycles` {REPEAT, REPEAT_OFFSET, MIRROR} √ó {before, after} √ó cycle-COUNT (0=‚àû), Cycles-modifier-must-be-first; the UI conflates both behind one "Extrapolation Mode" menu (Make Cyclic = secretly adds the modifier). Basher ORIGINALLY folded both into one per-side `extend` enum (D1), then **SPLIT them to match Blender (#275)**: hold/slope = the per-side extrapolation property, cycle family = the Cycles F-Modifier ‚Äî the "revisit the fold" is DONE. Near-term Basher gap surfaced = cycle COUNT (`cyclesBefore`/`cyclesAfter`, 0=‚àû, fall back to hold/slope past N). Blender ALSO keeps time-transport (NLA strip repeat / action cyclic-range = INTENT-ONLY) strictly separate from per-curve cycling ‚Äî grounds the "why not just loop the playhead range" question: range-loop can't do offset-travel / per-channel independence / render-time sampling); **D2** weighted, ordered multi-source layering, weight-is-a-channel (crossfade constraints, animation layers); **D3** deterministic multi-writer precedence (single-writer default; the id-keyed scan makes double-claim structurally easy ‚Üí scan-order render bug); **D4** per-sample enable gate (mute as a 0/1 channel ‚Äî generalizes C13); **D5** explicit sample-rate reconciliation (rises to HIGH with the fixed-30fps resample track); **D6** bake as explicit reversible op; **D7** stateful/temporal ops as a distinct contract-bound class (spring/lag secondary motion); **D8** explicit inter-frame feedback primitive (extends C6). Constraint sub-axes an aim-only example hid ([[V45]]/`CONSTRAINTS.md`): I7 track/up axis PARAMETERS (Basher hardcodes ‚àíZ/+Y), I8 up-vector modes, I9 maintain-offset/rest, I10 continuous weight (Basher has binary mute), I11 multi-constraint stacking by order+weight (Basher first-wins), + the constraint-TYPE generalization (resolver returns a TRS channel-mask so a future Parent/Point/Path reuses the seam, not touch every consumer).

**Breaks when:** an overlay resolves its target by walking the render/scene tree (N6 ‚Üí silent no-op at depth ‚Äî the live bug); the overlay finds the node but registers no dependency edge (N2 ‚Üí silent stale receiver); two overlays claim one (node,param) with no total order (D3 ‚Üí scan-order flicker); a stateful op is forced through the point-in-time path (C9 ‚Üí scrub‚âÝplayback); a channel samples outside its domain with no extend rule (D1 ‚Üí seam pop / blank scrub); a second constraint type assumes rotation-only overlay (‚Üí organizational fatality, touches every consumer). Type: STRUCTURAL+DATA-FLOW (edge-less overlay; two-graph resolution).
